    Changelog (Developer / Technical)¶

    Full technical detail for each release. Companion to CHANGELOG.md — same section structure, same entry numbering, same bold lead per entry, but the body keeps class names, file paths, audit IDs, error fingerprints, and failed-approaches notes that get trimmed from the user-facing log.

    Lift from commit-message bodies on each release; this file is a curated rollup, not new authoring.

    Legend: 🟢 confirmed working in-app  ·  🔴 added but not yet verified in-app

    [Unreleased]¶

    Verification session 2026-07-21: the open entries above/below were self-verified in-app via a scripted GUI Blender 5.2.0 session against the registered extension (probes + screenshots + full state restore; artifacts in gitignored dev/temp/verify_results.json, verify_shot_*.png, verify_corpus_leaks.json). Highlights: i18n corpus 6790 registered pairs — 6685 resolve to our German, 101 to Blender's own German (native catalog wins on common operator labels), 4 to Blender-owned identity-English editor terms ("Graph Editor" et al.), 0 English fallbacks of addon text; live tooltip pool: 463/464 operators + 53/53 menus draw descriptions that are verbatim texts/ constants, 0 trailing periods; autokey-guard state machine (ASK → consent → borrow → restore → manual-override WITHDRAW) exercised through the real operators with a live German report; tks.datablock_add_slot end-to-end slots 0→1; live bpy.utils.manual_map() resolves both guard ops to interface/navigation_panel/#autokey-is-being-blocked (anchor confirmed on the deployed wiki). Caveats: the consent-popup pixels and nav-warning visuals rest on the earlier in-app pass (d47b636); the guard-buttons grey-out branch (Fixed 5) is unreachable in a healthy session and stays covered by its unit tests.

    Added¶

    1. 🟢 The addon registers per-locale word lists with Blender's translation system — interface strings follow the user's Blender language. (In-app confirmed 2026-07-18 in Blender 5.2: "Kontext" panel title + "Ruhezustand" prefs accordion from our seed; note TKS_PT_Globals is poll-gated behind tks_show_tab_globals, so "Globals" is no verification anchor.) Multi-language support Phase 1. texts/i18n.py: build_dict() assembles {locale: {(context, source): translation}} from texts/locales/ (data modules; de_DE.py starter seed — Globals, Context, Batch Render, Value Lock, Rest State, Variant Switch, Render Presets, UI Sync; the Globals/Context N-panel headers are the visible verification anchors — the feature-group names are overlay runtime strings that stay English until the Phase 3 pgettext pass, and every tks.batch_render draw site overrides its label text); register_translations()/unregister_translations() default the registration name to the root package (__package__.rsplit), hooked early in root __init__.py register()/unregister() beside manual_map, plus _reload_order entries. Static RNA strings (bl_label, bl_description, prop name=/description=, enum item names) auto-translate in C at draw time — zero code changes, zero Python draw cost; dynamic strings (report(), drawn labels) are Phase 3 pgettext work. Verified 5.1 semantics: duplicate register raises ValueError (drives the refresh path), unregister of unknown names is a silent no-op. Tests: dev/tests/test_i18n_plumbing.py (5 — dict shape, real-string seed, name-scoped register/unregister roundtrip, reentrancy, root-init wiring guard). Suite gotcha documented in doc/troubleshooting/i18n_suite_source_tree_registration.md: collection-time module-level addon_enable in test_bookmark_channel_visibility.py enables the SOURCE-TREE addon, keeping a second registration alive — never assert global translation absence in-suite. Commit 2e45691.
    2. 🟢 Internal: i18n string collector (dev/scripts/i18n_extract.py). Phase 2. Pure-stdlib AST walk over the addon tree harvesting bl_label/bl_description assigns, name=/description= kwargs on *Property(...) calls, enum items= tuple slots 1–2, text= kwargs, and pgettext*() first args; identifiers (bl_idname, tokens, data paths) excluded by design. Yields 1818 unique strings across 2830 sites on main; coverage(catalog, locale_entries) splits translated/missing per locale (de_DE 5/1813 at seed stage — the Phase 5 guard test drives off this). CLI: python dev/scripts/i18n_extract.py takes_for_blender --locale de_DE [--json out]. Tests: dev/tests/test_i18n_extract.py (4). Same commit.
    3. 🟢 German N-panel batch — the side-panel surface renders in de_DE. Phase 4 batch 1: ~50 entries in texts/locales/de_DE.py covering panel/menu bl_labels (panel titles, tab + section headers, list-settings menus, keyframe pies, common action words). Static RNA strings only — no code changes, Blender's C draw layer does the lookup. Coverage 52/1823 harvested strings; the rest is the accepted backlog in the pending ledger. Commit 9e11d2d.
    4. 🟢 i18n wording-drift guard (dev/tests/test_i18n_guard.py) + generated pending ledger. Phase 5. Four headless tests over two new collector helpers — orphans(catalog, entries) (a locale key whose English source is gone → the label was reworded/removed and that translation silently died) and untracked(catalog, entries, keep_english, pending) (a harvested string that is neither translated, nor declared English-by-design, nor baselined → new wording with no i18n decision), plus dead-entry and translated-and-still-pending consistency checks. texts/locales/_pending.py is GENERATED (i18n_extract.py --write-pending, 1770 entries) and carries the hand-maintained KEEP_ENGLISH set, preserved across regenerations; it lets the guard be strict immediately instead of waiting for full coverage. Collector gained _POSITIONAL_TEXT_CALLS (register_feature_group(id, LABEL, icon)) — without it the orphan direction reported the live "UI Sync" string as dead. Full suite 1235 passed (Blender 5.2). Mirrored addon-side by auditor rule INFO-10 Translation Coverage (blender-addon-auditor commit 357c46f) so the same drift shows up in /stats scans and the dashboard. Same commit 9e11d2d. (Self-verified 2026-07-19 by GUI screenshot in Blender 5.2 — see Fixed entry for the operator-context follow-up that the screenshot exposed.)
    5. 🟢 German word list batch 2 — all short static strings (86.1% coverage). ~1,950 new texts/locales/de_DE.py entries covering every short static string (prefs labels, section headers, buttons, enum names, list menus, warnings, short tooltips): 2009 of 2334 harvested strings translated, backlog 2282→283 (mid-length + paragraph tooltips). KEEP_ENGLISH triage (42): token syntax examples/placeholders, log-topic labels (grep-ability), keyboard modifier names, brand/file identifiers, internal-only prop descriptions. Drift guard green — zero orphans, so every authored source string matches the code exactly. Full suite 1242 passed (5.2). Self-verified in-app by GUI screenshot: Baumansicht / Stempel-Notiz / Verzeichnis render in the live UI. Commit 8cb3bc0.

    6. 🟢 Autokey Availability Guard — the Autokey button manages Blender's "Only Insert Available" preference, consent-gated. Blender 5.2 defaults preferences.edit.use_keyframe_insert_available to ON, which makes autokey silently insert nothing on never-keyed channels — and every fresh take starts that way (root cause of the fresh-install "autokey doesn't work" report; doc/troubleshooting/autokey_blender52_only_insert_available.md). New core/autokey_guard.py: pure guard_decision → WITHDRAW/ASK/TAKE/RELEASE/NONE plus take_ownership/release_ownership/withdraw/take_if_consented; tks.toggle_autokey borrows the pref on enable and restores it on disable. One-time consent popup (tks.autokey_guard_accept / tks.autokey_guard_decline; decline flips the new automation pref autokey_manage_insert_available — default True, Preferences → Workflow → Autokey — off instead of hiding state); popup is guarded with bpy.app.background — wm.popup_menu ACCESS-VIOLATES headless even when context.window is truthy. Hand-editing the pref in native Preferences withdraws consent (lazy detection, never fought in the same tick). Value Lock and Rest State Mode release the borrow when they pause autokey and silently re-take it (consented + autokey actually on) on restore. Fallback nav warning system_autokey_blocked.py (accept/decline; hidden for good after decline) for autokey enabled via Blender's own button; condition is_autokey_blocked is boolean-reads-only, imports hoisted in panel.py after the ARCH-04 gate flagged the deferred-import hot path. Props +4 (autokey_manage_insert_available, autokey_manage_consented, autokey_available_borrowed, expand_auto_autokey), EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 527→531; prefs-search section "Autokey". Rest-Mode constrained-editing phases (pref inverted ON inside the mode + flat-frame-0) remain open on the roadmap card. Tests: dev/tests/test_autokey_guard.py (13 — decision matrix, take/release, override withdrawal, consent ops); full suite 1205 passed. Commit 9b50b92. First in-app pass caught a display gap: is_autokey_blocked required not borrowed, which is exactly the manual-override state (borrow held + blocker flipped back ON by hand), so the ask-again warning never returned until the next toggle — fixed by dropping the term (managed-fine still hides via the blocker reading OFF, decline via manage=False) plus an override-specific paragraph in the warning via the new public is_manual_override() (a private _addon_prefs import from panels would have been ARCH-03); +5 visibility-matrix tests, suite 1210 passed. Commit d47b636.

    7. 🟢 German word list completed — PENDING 686 → 0. texts/locales/de_DE.py 2009 → 2695 entries; the 42 KEEP_ENGLISH strings (identifiers, brand terms, format literals) remain English by design, so every translatable catalog string now resolves. Translated to the conventions in the file header (Ansichtsebene / Voreinstellung / Kaskade / Ruhezustand / Wertsperre / Datenblock / Strg+Klick; Take, Slot, Keyframe, Frame, Viewport, Override, Token, Tag, Pie stay English). Bulk of the batch was the 403 operator tooltips that phase 3 of the texts/ centralization had just made harvestable. Process: work list keyed BY INDEX against a dumped pending.json, never by re-typed source text — the drift guard keys on exact English source, and a console round-trip mangles UTF-8. Pre-merge validator (scratch merge_de.py) asserted per entry: identical newline count, preserved leading/trailing whitespace, identical placeholder set ({}/%s/[token]/<Data>), and no untranslated domain term; it refuses to write on any failure. Five real defects caught and fixed rather than forced through: {curly} mistranslated to {geschweiften} (it demonstrates literal brace syntax); one entry using informal 'du'; three tooltips quoting English button names ('Preload View Layers', 'Storage') that ARE translated, so they referenced labels absent from a German UI; and 'Exclude from View Layer' — Blender's own Outliner label, which Blender translates — now 'Von Ansichtsebene ausschließen'. _pending.py regenerated to 0. Suite 1359 passed on Blender 5.2 including test_i18n_guard.py. Commit 3f86940.

    8. 🟢 Runtime-composed strings: cascade pilot batch migrated to template-then-format. Phase 3. 29 f-string text= sites across operators/cascade/ (override/base popover headings, link warnings, purge rows, picker menu items) reworked to pgettext_iface("Action Override for '%s'") % vl.name. Helpers are canonical RE-EXPORTS in texts/i18n.py (pgettext_iface/_rpt/_tip) — the collector and auditor INFO-10 key on the exact function name at the call site, an alias would hide every template from the drift guard. New dev/scripts/i18n_triage.py classifies all 593 composed sites (110 user-readable; 476 number/path glue skipped as no_words; JSON drives the remaining batches: panels/navigation 16, operators/inspector 12, operators/misc 9, features/* ~25, reports TBD). 22 German template entries (word order moves around the placeholder: Rename '%s' → '%s' umbenennen); pending ledger regenerated to 0. 4 tests in dev/tests/test_i18n_runtime.py incl. a no-composed-text-left guard over the migrated area. Full suite 1303 passed (5.2); template resolution verified headless via the registered extension. Commit 012bd0e.
    9. 🟢 Phase 3 complete — all 83 remaining composed sites migrated + whole-tree guard. 46 files: batch-render/preset dialogs, smart-syntax pickers, variant/still popovers, inspector action+slot dialogs, slot-cleanup confirmations, tag library, render-queue header, every navigation warning header, preferences data tools. Plural headers become EXPLICIT singular/plural templates ("%d Cascade Drift" / "%d Cascade Drifts") instead of an inline {'s' if n != 1} suffix — a translator inflects the whole phrase (verified: 1 Kaskaden-Abweichung / 3 Kaskaden-Abweichungen). The report() site uses pgettext_rpt so Blender's separate Translate Reports pref still governs it. test_no_translatable_fstrings_left_in_cascade_ops is replaced by test_no_translatable_composed_strings_left_anywhere, which imports dev/scripts/i18n_triage.py and reuses its classify() — guard and triage cannot disagree, and any new UI f-string fails the suite with file/line/text. 87 German templates; pending ledger 0; coverage 98.8% (41 English-by-design). Full suite 1310 passed (5.2). Commit b9ddca0.

    Changed¶

    1. 🟢 Internal: removed the orphan get_entries_for_id helper from the rest cache — no behavior change. Auditor MAINT-01 (orphan top-level functions): features/rest_state/rest_cache.py::get_entries_for_id lost its only caller when the rest-revert evidence-gate fix removed revert_snap's rest-cache fallback (Fixed entry 1, commit 69ba211); verified zero callers on main — the remaining references on the stale feat/* worktree branches predate that fix, so a merge takes main's caller-free revert_snap.py. Full suite 1294 passed / 0 failed post-removal. Commit 62eecac.
    2. 🟢 Internal: test_undo_removes_object is locale-agnostic — no behavior change. The test asserted the hardcoded English name "Cube" after primitive_cube_add, which fails on installations where Blender translates new data names (German UI creates "Würfel" — surfaced once the i18n pilot put the dev machine on de_DE). The add is now detected via the IDSnapshot delta, the same mechanism the test's undo assertion already uses. Commit 348bd33.

    3. 🟢 Internal: draw_wrapped_paragraph honors manual line breaks — no visible change until a text uses one. New pure seam ui/styles.py::split_paragraphs: \n in an INFOBOX_* constant starts a new wrapped line, a blank line becomes a paragraph gap (separator(factor=1.2)), blank runs collapse, and whitespace-only text still draws nothing — the empty-body wrapped_info_box call in the autokey-blocked warning depends on that. Authors control info-box layout from texts/infoboxes.py without touching draw code (previously wrap_measured's text.split() swallowed newlines like spaces). 4 tests beside the other wrap tests in test_naming_validation.py; suite 1214 passed. Commit c5d756c.

    4. 🟢 Internal: phase 1 of the texts/ centralization campaign — 18 sites migrated, plus the tool that does it. New dev/scripts/apply_text_centralization.py: reads the auditor's INFO-09 rows (kind / file / line / target module), lifts the literal at each site via AST anchors, appends NAME = <text verbatim> to the destination texts/ module and rewrites the site to reference it, adding or extending the relative import. Dry-run by default; --kind / --area scope a batch; already-migrated sites are skipped so re-runs are no-ops. Phase 1 cleared bl_description (9 → 0) and the static infobox_literal sites (11 → 2; the 2 survivors are f-strings needing a template constant): 18 constants across infoboxes.py, tooltips_preferences.py, tooltips_misc.py, tooltips_batch_render.py, tooltips_render_presets.py. Two tool bugs caught by tests before they shipped: (a) Blender's property syntax is an ANNOTATION (prop: BoolProperty(...)), so the Call hangs off .annotation not .value — every prop_desc constant would otherwise be named PROP_<CLASS> with no property segment; (b) the texts import must be placed after the last top-level import located via AST — a line-scan inserted INSIDE a parenthesised multi-line import and split it (features/smart_syntax/registry.py). Multi-line implicit-concat literals are now refused outright (splicing head+name+tail across the span drops the separating comma — it produced invalid Python at registry.py:662 on the first run) and reported for hand migration. 15 tool tests in dev/tests/test_text_centralization_tool.py; full suite 1341 passed on Blender 5.2; auditor re-scan 619 → 601 findings with orphans unchanged at 31 (a rewrite that stranded a constant would show up there). Remaining: 196 prop_desc, 403 op_docstring (phase 4 — ADD bl_description, keep __doc__), 2 f-strings, 31 orphans. Plan: dev/plan_text_centralization.md. Commit bd698c9.

    5. 🟢 Internal: phase 2 — 143 single-line property descriptions centralized (prop_desc). Same REPLACE mode as phase 1: the description= literal at each property definition becomes a PROP_* constant in the matching texts module and the site references it. INFO-09 prop_desc 196 → 53 (the multi-line remainder closed in Changed entry 9). Commit 4ae54c2. (Backfilled — this mirror entry was missed when the user-facing entry landed in e0854e5.)

    6. 🟢 Internal: the i18n collector harvests texts/ module constants. dev/scripts/i18n_extract.py walked draw/property/operator sites only, so a centralized string went invisible the moment migration replaced its literal with a constant reference — roughly 500 already-centralized strings were missing from the catalog. The collector now walks the texts/ package's module-level string assigns as first-class sources; _pending.py regenerated to record the newly-visible strings. Commits db2638e, 0199796. (Backfilled, same gap as entry 5.)

    7. 🟢 Internal: phase 3 — 403 operator tooltips centralized (op_docstring). Blender promotes cls.__doc__ to the tooltip only while bl_description is absent, so 403 operators were shipping their developer docstring as user-facing UI. New ADD mode in dev/scripts/apply_text_centralization.py: instead of replacing a literal it inserts bl_description = OP_<NAME> directly after bl_idname at matching indentation and copies the RAW docstring value (ast.get_docstring(clean=True) re-indents, which would silently change the tooltip); the docstring stays for developers. Idempotent — skips classes already declaring bl_description, and those with no docstring (nothing to move). 403 constants across 9 texts modules (195 → tooltips_misc; splitting that module by area stays open), 109 files. Verified NAMESPACE-AWARE: each of the 403 constants resolved through its own file's import and compared to that class's docstring — 0 wrong tooltips. (A flat cross-module check first reported 2 false mismatches: OP_VLVVARIANTPOPOVER and OP_RENAMEITEM legitimately exist in two modules with different text; each site imports the correct one and no module defines a name twice.) Two follow-up fixes in 240e456: (a) the import must land after the HEADER import block, not the last import in the file — features/bookmarks/operators.py carries a second block at line 222, so the constant was referenced at class-body evaluation before its import ran (NameError → whole feature failed to register → 8 cascading failures); a repair pass over all 109 files found it as the only case, and a regression test drives the shape. (b) The i18n guard correctly flagged 403 untracked strings: the collector harvests texts/ but not docstrings, so centralizing made these tooltips translatable for the first time — _pending.py regenerated 283 → 686. Suite 1359 passed on Blender 5.2; 23 tool tests. Commits 1daa91f, 240e456.

    8. 🟢 All 53 menu docstring-tooltips centralized + translated. A bpy.types.Menu promotes its class docstring to the hover tooltip exactly like an Operator (verified: Menu.bl_rna carries bl_description on 5.2), but the INFO-09 op_docstring detector only matched Operator bases, so all 53 Takes menus were shipping developer docstrings as user-facing UI the i18n collector never harvested — the German pilot showed them in English (the reported N-panel Add-menu tooltip). Fixed both sides: auditor extends INFO-09 to Operator OR Menu (blender-addon-auditor 1d98f13); Takes centralizes the 53 via the migration tool. Tool bug found + fixed by the namespace-aware verify: const_name ignored the class type infix, so TKS_MT_CreateRenderPreset and TKS_OT_CreateRenderPreset both minted OP_CREATERENDERPRESET — a duplicate in one module (last wins) that gave the operator the menu's text (4 operators wrong on the first run). const_name now prefixes by infix: MENU_<suffix> for TKS_MT_*, OP_<suffix> for operators (unchanged); regression test locks it. Post-fix: 53/53 menus resolve to their own docstring, no duplicate constants. Then translated to German (de_DE 2696 → 2749; PENDING 53 → 0). 27 files, 53 constants across 6 texts modules; 26 tool tests. Suite 1369 passed on Blender 5.2. Commits 49aaab8, fe36037. NB: the 'Icon: ADD' line in the reported screenshot is Blender's own Developer Extras output (the pref was enabled), not addon text — the menu is drawn icon='ADD'.

    9. 🟢 INFO-09 prop_desc backlog closed — 51 multi-line property descriptions centralized. These used implicit string concatenation across lines; the migration tool had blanket-refused multi-line literals after the positional wrapped_info_box splice bug. A description= is a BOUNDED kwarg, so its multi-line form replaces cleanly — the skip is now narrowed to infobox_literal only, plus a self-protecting whole-file ast.parse backstop that reverts a file rather than write it broken. 51 constants / 5 modules / 20 files. NO new translation: the collector harvests description= literals from code directly (unlike docstrings), so these were already in the catalog and translated — PENDING stays 0. Verified 0 duplicate constants, all refs resolve, suite 1373 passed. 3 tool tests (27 total). Remaining INFO-09: 5 f-string sites (form: dynamic) that need the template-restructure of the runtime-message i18n phase. Commit 71b9c05.
    10. 🟢 INFO-09 closed to 0 — the 5 f-string tooltips centralized as templates. Runtime-assembled description=f"…" / wrapped_info_box(f"…") sites can't be plain constants, so they became named TEMPLATE constants filled via .format(): 3 per-tier override descriptions (PROP_TIER_OVERRIDE_{VL,SCENE,GLOBAL} in tooltips_render_presets, {field} from the _TIER_PRESET_FIELDS loop) and 2 storage-status info boxes (INFOBOX_STORAGE_{PROJECT_PREFS_MISSING,TIER_FALLBACK}, {path}/{msg} runtime values). The info-box sites are also fully translatable — the call site does pgettext_iface(TEMPLATE).format(...) (translate the template, THEN interpolate; texts/i18n.py rule), verified under de_DE. All 5 templates translated (de_DE 2750→2755, PENDING 0). Suite 1376 passed. INFO-09 now 0 (was 56 at session start). NB the 3 property-description templates are centralized but not display-translated by Blender (it matches the interpolated result, not the template) — acceptable for these advanced tier fields; full translation would need per-field enumeration. Commit 4a63f3c.
    11. 🟢 Internal: all 651 operator.report() messages routed through pgettext_rpt. Blender auto-translates RNA metadata but never report() output, so every status/error line was untranslatable. New transform tool dev/scripts/wrap_report_i18n.py (14 tests): a literal becomes pgettext_rpt("…"); an f-string becomes pgettext_rpt(template).format(fields) — template-first per the texts/i18n.py rule; conversions and format-specs are refused for hand migration. AST col offsets are UTF-8 BYTE offsets, so all source splicing is done in bytes (an em-dash earlier in the line otherwise ate a closing paren; the self-protecting whole-file re-parse caught it before writing). Auditor INFO-11 (blender-addon-auditor 2fc2f30) counts unwrapped report literals: 651 → 0. Suite 1404 passed. Commit e607e88. (Backfilled — mirror entry missed when 0e6bece landed the user-facing line.)
    12. 🟢 Internal: the 525 report templates translated to German. de_DE 2756 → 3281, PENDING 0. Placeholder sets, newline counts and trailing whitespace validated before merge — a dropped {field} would raise KeyError at .format() time in production. Verified live under de_DE: "No view layers found to render" → "Keine Ansichtsebenen zum Rendern gefunden"; the templated "{label} cancelled ({elapsed:.1f}s)" renders "Background Render abgebrochen (3.2s)". Commits f875f9b, 6118155. (Backfilled, same gap as entry 11.)
    13. 🟢 Whole-corpus wording/format polish — 353 of 1179 texts/ strings changed, German re-keyed in lockstep. Mechanical pipeline over every constant in the 15 texts/ modules: tooltips drop the trailing period (Blender's own API lint convention; info boxes keep theirs as prose), docstring-migration artifacts removed (indented line wraps joined mid-sentence, blank lines collapsed, double spaces squeezed — deliberate modifier lines like Alt+Click: … keep their own line), migration mojibake fixed (=2 → "at least two", ? → →, --/-> → em dash/arrow), terminology unified (ViewLayer → View Layer in prose, Unassign, Alt+Click casing, US spellings). On top, 93 hand rewrites where internal rationale had leaked into user-facing tooltips (picker dispatch-chain notes, keymap segfault explanations, "Currently dormant since v0.5" markers, "Phase 4" placeholders, F12_PIE_SLOT_ITEMS enum ids). de_DE.py re-keyed by English msgid in the same commit — 260 entries migrated mechanically with the same formatting rules, 92 retranslated to match the rewrites, 1 previously-untranslated string added (3282 entries, PENDING 0, missing-count strictly below main's baseline). Suite 1411 passed on Blender 5.2. Commit e47e3cd.

    Fixed¶

    1. 🟢 Rest-revert snap is now evidence-gated on witnessed key loss (trap-state enforcement + wrong-place snap). _revert_unkeyed_to_rest_deferred (features/rest_state/revert_snap.py) snapped every user of a modified take action whose channels were unkeyed at the current frame — so an object left in the "action assigned, slot empty" state by Clear Keyframes / Alt+I was yanked to rest ~0.1 s after every subsequent autokey-off move (value-lock-like enforcement; the autokey-off early-exit path in mirror_logic.py queues the revert on ANY transform of an action-bearing object), and all 13 users of the shared take were swept as collateral (field log 2026-07-14 12:22). The snap could also land in the WRONG place: the hand-rolled slot matcher missed short-form/pipe slot names and silently fell back to the live rest cache — selection-time live snapshots, not rest values. Fix: per-target key-count baseline (_slot_key_counts, seeded seed-only from rest_cache._snapshot_id_block, cleared via clear_key_count_cache() in invalidate_and_rebuild() on undo/redo/file-load) — a target snaps only when its assigned slot's keyframe count DECREASED since last observation; rest values now resolve through the shared _resolve_rest_slot + _snap_one_target path (same source as the drift scanner and apply_rest_values, keyed-anywhere protection), and the rest-cache fallback is removed (uncovered targets skip with a logged warning). The original count-based drift detection (auto_snap_keyframe_clear.md) had been lost in the rest_state_snap_on_keyframe_delete.md rework. 9 regression tests in dev/tests/test_revert_snap_evidence.py; full suite 1294 passed. Troubleshooting: doc/troubleshooting/rest_revert_trap_state_snapping.md. Commit 69ba211.
    2. 🟢 auto_snap_on_clear preference wired up. Defined/drawn/search-indexed since its introduction but never consumed by the snap path. New _auto_snap_enabled() (default True, True when prefs unavailable) gates the snap portion of _revert_unkeyed_to_rest_deferred; the rest-cache invalidation on rest-action authoring (Fixed entry 1's sibling concern, guarded by test_gate_off_still_invalidates_rest_cache) deliberately runs regardless of the pref. Same commit 69ba211.

    3. 🟢 Datablock popover "New Slot" button no longer dies on a stale slots.new(for_id=) call. TKS_OT_DatablockAddSlot.execute (operators/inspector/ops_datablock_action.py) still used the pre-4.4 draft signature action.slots.new(for_id=target), which raises TypeError: ActionSlots.new(): required parameter "id_type" not specified on every Blender 5.x — the call was unguarded, so the button always failed with a Python error; every other slot-creation site had already been migrated to (id_type, name). Found during the 2026-07-16 autokey audit (fresh 0.7.11 install on a second PC) and confirmed by live probe on 5.1.2. Fix derives both parameters through the canonical helpers — core.anim_utils.resolve_id_type + core.path_utils.derive_slot_name_for_target — so the slot label follows the user's naming template instead of a raw datablock name (the animation_data_loss_fresh_install.md lesson). Regression test dev/tests/test_datablock_add_slot.py drives the operator end-to-end (RED: TypeError at the old call; GREEN after). Troubleshooting: doc/troubleshooting/datablock_add_slot_stale_api.md. Commit 96ec131.

    4. 🟢 Autokey-guard operators had no MANUAL_MAP entry (right-click → Online Manual dead-ended at the wiki home). tks.autokey_guard_accept / tks.autokey_guard_decline (operators/ui/ops_misc_ui.py:68,93) are drawn from the Toggle-Autokey consent popup and the Autokey Is Being Blocked nav warning (panels/navigation/warnings/system_autokey_blocked.py), but carried no explicit map row, so only the catch-all wildcard matched and the manual link resolved to (wiki home). Surfaced by the auditor's INFO-01 manual_map_audit as two routing findings once the operators became documented (wiki eee4c37 added the Autokey Is Being Blocked section to interface/navigation_panel.md — itself the fix for the two coverage_audit findings). Fix: two manual overrides in doc/reports/data/wire_assignments.json → interface/navigation_panel/#autokey-is-being-blocked, then dev/scripts/apply_wire_assignments.py regenerated the AUTO-WIRED block (971 → 973 rows; diff is exactly the two new rows — the generator was fed a fresh codebase_stats.json copied from the auditor, since a stale/absent input would rewrite the whole block). Resolution verified against Blender's matcher semantics (lowercase id → case-sensitive fnmatchcase → first match wins) and the all-patterns-lowercase invariant; -k manual_map subset 28 passed on Blender 5.2. Note: codebase_stats.json is a 1.7 MB transient pipeline input and is deliberately NOT committed. Commit 644dc7d.

    5. 🟢 TKS_OT_AutokeyGuardAccept / TKS_OT_AutokeyGuardDecline had no poll() (CORR-07 missing: 2). Both shipped with the 2026-07-16 autokey-guard work without a precondition, so the buttons stayed clickable when context.preferences.addons.get(ADDON_MODULE) could not resolve — execute() then returned {'CANCELLED'} with no report, i.e. a dead click. The auditor classified them as REAL rather than by-design (its harmless: 304 bucket already excuses the INTERNAL-by-design set). Fix: both now poll() on exactly what execute() needs — reachable addon preferences, since accept writes autokey_manage_insert_available / autokey_manage_consented and decline clears them. The duplicated lookup is extracted to a module-level _guard_prefs(context) and ADDON_MODULE hoisted to a module-level import (core.constants is a leaf re-export; poll runs on every redraw of the autokey-blocked warning panel, so it must not sit behind a deferred import — ARCH-04 / draw-path cost). Deliberately NOT a UI-state poll: the system_autokey_blocked panel draws the buttons unconditionally, and that panel only exists while the addon is registered, so the preferences always resolve there and the buttons never grey out in practice. Registered in the existing CORR-07 registry dev/tests/test_corr07_polls.py (AST-based, mirrors the auditor's own parse). Suite 1341 → 1343 passed on Blender 5.2; re-scan CORR-07 missing 2 → 0, quality 9.9 → 10.0. Commit 86d117e.

    6. 🟢 Word-list entries are mirrored into Blender's operator translation context. Button labels stayed English while panel headers translated: Blender resolves layout.operator(text=…) labels in contexts.operator_default ("Operator"), but bl_label / panel headers use the default '*' context, so entries authored only under '*' never reached any button (the Context / Inspector tabs were the visible case; translation misses never error, so it read as "i18n is broken"). Root-caused by a GUI probe in Blender 5.2 — registering the same sources under the operator context made the tabs render marker text, the '*' entry alone never did. texts/i18n.py::build_dict() now mirrors each default-context entry into the operator context (translators still author one line per string); a hand-authored operator-context entry wins over the mirror. 2 tests in dev/tests/test_i18n_plumbing.py; troubleshooting doc/troubleshooting/i18n_operator_context_buttons.md. Commit ff39176.

    7. 🟢 The custom-token preset row now mirrors styles.preset_row — native search popup + [+][✏][X] cluster. The picker (features/smart_syntax/presets.py) was a bpy.types.Menu (TKS_MT_custom_token_presets) drawing one row(align=True) per preset with an inline X; a Menu lays children in an implicit single column, so a row() per entry made Blender reflow into a second column — the delete buttons and the trailing "Save current tokens as…" broke away from the list (reported from a German-UI screenshot). First rebuilt as an INSTANCED popover panel (2a38b4e); that fixed the reflow but still didn't match the Properties preset rows, which use styles.preset_row (ui/preset_rows.py) — a native invoke_search_popup selector plus a [tier][badge][name][+ create][✏ edit][X] cluster. Parity pass (c3bad58): the popover panel is replaced by TKS_OT_SearchCustomTokenPreset, mirroring TKS_OT_SearchRenderPreset — bl_property = "preset_name", a dynamic enum built from list_presets(tier) and retained through utils.enum_cache.retain (a runtime os.listdir-derived enum dangles otherwise, per [[feedback_dynamic_enum_retain]]), invoke_search_popup in invoke, apply in execute. The row's ✏ is a new TKS_OT_EditCustomTokenPreset (rename + move-tier invoke_props_dialog, mirroring TKS_OT_EditRenderPreset; the tokens themselves are edited in the grid, so a preset needs an identity edit) — save-new/delete-old, and the selection follows the rename when it was active. Kept the single-tier listing (deliberate divergence from the render picker's all-tiers popover, per the user's earlier "filtered tier" call), so the tier dropdown stays meaningful. The dirty-driven +→✓ save / ✏→↩ revert toggles that preset_row also carries need token change-tracking that doesn't exist yet — deferred to the token-preset-ownership work (doc/roadmap/ideas/token-preset-ownership.md). Cleanup: the interim popover's custom_token_preset_filter StringProperty removed (native search has its own field), EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT reverted 532 → 531, and the i18n word list reconciled (2 orphans dropped, 4 new strings translated). 10 tests in dev/tests/test_token_preset_selector.py; full suite 1258 passed on Blender 5.2. Troubleshooting doc/troubleshooting/token_preset_picker_menu_reflow.md. Commits 2a38b4e, c3bad58.

    8. 🟢 Info-box bodies stayed English in a translated UI — wrapped before translated. ui/styles.py::draw_wrapped_paragraph split the source into per-line fragments and drew each via col.label(); Blender only translates a label equal to a COMPLETE registered msgid, so a wrapped fragment matched nothing and the registered German was never applied (reported on the Custom Tokens info box). Fix: one bpy.app.translations.pgettext_iface(text) on the whole string before wrapping (the template-first rule texts/i18n.py documents), hoisted above the wrap loop (perf rule); fragments drawn with translate=False. The box header was already fine (whole-string label). Single wrap path ⇒ fixes every info box. Behaviorally verified: pgettext_iface on the real Custom Tokens string returns 'Eigene Token aus Szenendaten definieren …' under de_DE. 3 source-contract tests; test_info_box fake layout updated to accept the translate kwarg. Suite 1376 passed. Commit beb1a09.
    9. 🟢 FG batch render start crashed Blender 5.2 with EXCEPTION_ACCESS_VIOLATION — the render_stats registration is now version-gated. Blender 5.2 added BKE_callback_exec_string(G_MAIN, rs->infostr, BKE_CB_EVT_RENDER_STATS) to the UI render job's image_renderinfo_cb (render_internal.cc) WITHOUT the rs->infostr == nullptr early-return the background path (stats_update, pipeline.cc) has; at the first stats draw of do_render_full_pipeline infostr is still NULL, and with ANY Python handler in bpy.app.handlers.render_stats the bridge crashes in PyC_UnicodeFromBytes → strlen(NULL) on the render thread BEFORE Python runs (fingerprint: strlen ← PyC_UnicodeFromBytes ← bpy_app_generic_callback ← BKE_callback_exec_string ← image_renderinfo_cb ← do_render_full_pipeline). The handler's defensive *args signature never helped — the C bridge only early-outs when the handler LIST is empty, which is also why vanilla Blender doesn't crash. Source-verified: 5.1-release has no exec call there; upstream main still unguarded (report draft: dev/temp/blender_bugreport_render_stats_null.md). Fix: render_hooks.fg_render_stats_supported() (False on ≥ 5.2.0 until the upstream guard lands) gates the FG append AND its register_process("FG Render Stats Handler") row in operators.py invoke; cleanup stays unconditional (idempotent removal, unregister_process no-ops on unknown names). FG per-VL progress falls back to the elapsed-based estimate — the effective 5.x behavior anyway (FG render_stats only ever delivered the final Time: line, per doc/roadmap/_dev/render-eta-precision.md). The headless BG worker (cli_worker.py) keeps its handler — the BG stats path NULL-guards. Tests: dev/tests/test_render_stats_52_gate.py (4 — version matrix, live-version default, registration-site-gated source guard); full suite 1321 passed on Blender 5.2. Troubleshooting: doc/troubleshooting/render_stats_null_infostr_crash_52.md. Commit 4295c3e.

    1. 🟢 Automatic View-Layer Preload can open the progress panel for you.     2. 🟢 The public wiki now mirrors the changelog, alongside the roadmap.     4. 🟢 Quick-insert tokens + Clear Last / Clear All in every token field's ▾ popover. Each field's ▾ popover (the naming-template rows and the Smart Output Directory / File Name rows) gained an "Insert Token" list of its top essential tokens — one click appends the bracketed token at the very end of the field — plus "Clear Last Token" (drops the last whole token via the shared parse_segments/remove_segment, never a single character) and "Clear All" (empties the field). The list is the field's valid tokens only, so a click can never produce an invalid-token status: naming rows rank essential_tokens_for_field(field) (preferences/naming.py, intersected with TOKENS_PER_TEMPLATE, date/time excluded, cap 5); output rows rank essential_tokens_for_filter('CONTEXT','RENDER_PATH') against the new shared ESSENTIAL_TOKEN_PRIORITY (features/smart_syntax/builder.py). Wired through one pair of target-aware operators in builder.py — tks.field_append_token (reads target, appends format_token_for(mode, token)) and tks.field_clear (action CLEAR_LAST / CLEAR_ALL) — both keyed by the same (target_kind, target_data, bracket_mode) param set the Build Syntax launcher already uses, so prefs/CURLY (naming) and scene/SMART (output) share the code; this replaced two short-lived naming-only operators (tks.append_naming_token / tks.edit_naming_field) authored earlier the same session, avoiding duplicate operators. _draw_field_actions (naming) and the new _draw_quickpick_and_clear helper (features/batch_render/panel.py) draw the rows; Reset to Default was regrouped to sit just above the two clear rows so all "undo my edits" actions are together. Tests: test_output_popover_quickpick.py (new, Dir/File popover wiring), essential_tokens_for_filter cases in test_token_builder.py, the quick-pick/clear cases in test_naming_validation.py, and updated sequence/divider expectations in test_row_action_menu.py. Full suite 634 passed, 1 skipped. Lives in the new features/smart_syntax/ package (see Changed entry 7). ✅ in-app verified.

    5. 🟢 A search bar above the Preferences tabs dims non-matching settings (Naming tab pilot). Blender's native settings search is C-level and never reaches an AddonPreferences.draw() body — there is no API to read the native filter text and it won't dim custom rows — so the dim-non-matches / keep-matches-highlighted behaviour is reimplemented in Python. New prefs_search StringProperty on TKS_MiscPropsMixin (preferences/props/props_misc.py) with options={'TEXTEDIT_UPDATE','SKIP_SAVE'} and no update= callback (live redraw per keystroke; typing never triggers autosave); added to persistence_io.UI_STATE_KEYS so the JSON persistence never serializes it; EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 481→482. Two pure decision functions (unit-tested in isolation): pref_matches(query, *texts) in preferences/addon_prefs_helpers.py (case-insensitive substring; empty query → True; None-safe) and naming_search_flags(query, title, fields, label_fn=naming_field_label) in preferences/draw_naming.py (returns (section_match, {field: active}); a title hit lights the whole section; empty query is neutral so manual expand state is respected). Wiring: draw_naming_template_row gained active=True (sets row.active), draw_collapsible_section gained force_expand=False/active=True (search reveals a matching section without disturbing the stored expand flag and dims a no-match header), _draw_naming_categories/draw_naming_tab thread the query from prefs.prefs_search. Scope: Naming tab only (the data-driven NAMING_TEMPLATE_CATEGORIES pilot); the bar is global but other tabs are inline draws that opt in later (roadmap phase 4), and cross-tab auto-jump is deliberately out of scope. Tests: dev/tests/test_prefs_search.py (9, all pure); adjacent persistence/naming/panel/UI/accordion groups 116 passed. Roadmap doc/roadmap/active/prefs-search.md. ✅ in-app verified.

    12. 🟢 The Build Syntax popover flags a non-rooted render directory and offers Make Absolute / Make Relative. Appears ONLY when the target is a directory (is_directory_target: scene tks_render_directory or a File Output node's directory — not filenames, slot subpaths or naming templates). The popover: flags "Invalid Syntax" when the path isn't rooted — it must start with // (blend-relative) or an absolute path (drive C:/, POSIX /, UNC), else Blender saves to an unpredictable working-dir location (path_mode(text) == 'NEITHER'); bakes an abs/rel badge into the field icon (EVENT_A absolute / EVENT_R blend-relative, error glyph when not rooted); offers Make Absolute / Make Relative in the ▾ menu acting on the builder buffer (tks.toggle_render_path_mode target='builder'), greyed until saved.     13. 🟢 The Properties Output and File Output node directory fields show path invalidity directly. Directory validity (rooted // or absolute, no dangling separators) now shows on the live Properties-Output and File Output node directory fields, not just the popover: the field turns red (.alert on an inner row) and its badge becomes the error glyph when path_mode == 'NEITHER' (incl. empty); the preview box shows "Invalid Syntax — " in red instead of a bogus resolved path. The check was refactored into a shared string-based pattern_syntax_error(text, bmode, is_directory=); builder_syntax_error delegates to it. An empty directory is flagged too — the root-check runs before the empty short-circuit (path_mode('') == 'NEITHER'), so an empty dir reads "Invalid Syntax" and blocks Apply/Copy instead of "(nothing to resolve yet)"; filenames/naming templates still allow empty. Module-level _directory_error/_directory_badge_icon helpers in batch_render/panel.py are panel-draw-safe (never raise). Commits d3eb867, 260bb24.

    14. 🟢 The Build Syntax popover edits a private DRAFT — a red Apply flag beside the field is the only write path. REVISED 2026-07-12 (user decision, reversing this entry's earlier live write-through design, commits 7e6cc79/d340c82, which had been verified but proved wrong in use: every token click / chip edit leaked straight into the real field). The _builder_to_target update callback on tks_token_builder is removed — the buffer is isolated again. New pure builder_apply_state(draft, live, syntax_error) → HIDDEN (draft matches live) / READY (differs, valid → red flag via row.alert) / BLOCKED (differs, invalid syntax → grayed); the flag draws in the field row of draw_builder_strip between the field and the Browse/▾ controls, and tks.token_builder_apply (TKS_OT_BuilderApply, poll blocks on no-target or builder_syntax_error) performs the _write_target commit.     15. 🟢 The Build Syntax popover flags a leading / trailing / doubled separator as invalid syntax. A separator only makes sense BETWEEN two values, so a pattern that leads, trails, or doubles a separator (e.g. [sep][hostname] → "_NIWO") can't produce a usable name. New builder_syntax_error() detects this; when it fires the popover shows "Invalid Syntax — " (red) instead of the resolved name, hides Apply, and greys out Copy (and Apply) via their poll. 8 new tests. Commit f51b075.

    16. 🟢 The Build Syntax popover's ▾ menu offers Copy, Make Absolute/Relative, Reset to Default, Clear Last Token and Clear All. Built up over the session: Reset / Clear Last / Clear All added (2d72035), consolidated onto one row (c8057b0), then moved into a ▾ dropdown with Apply red only when the builder differs from its target (0fdc399), the Apply made icon-only + right-aligned beside the ▾ (1b2cd53, a0471c2). After two non-working approaches — a nested popover can't repaint the keep-open popup (Blender only refreshes a floating popup on the next mouse event), and the bpy.ops.wm.call_panel re-open workaround CRASHES Blender (uncatchable access violation when call_panel runs without a valid window) — the final form is a real Blender Menu TKS_MT_TokenBuilderActions drawn via field_row.menu() (Tree-View ➕ style), which closes cleanly and repaints the popup. The old INSTANCED popover Panel TKS_PT_TokenBuilderActions and _action_row helper were removed. Commits 2d72035, c8057b0, 0fdc399, 1b2cd53, a0471c2, 204173a, 8f75468. ✅ in-app verified.

    18. 🟢 The Context panel warns when a naming template has an invalid token, with one-click fixes and a default fallback. Two distinct red statuses, each with its own fix (warn-loudly, no auto-mutation): wrong FORMAT (ERROR icon — a token not in the required {curly} style, e.g. [scene]/<scene>/[scene}; classify_token_issues() detects these where the old get_invalid_tokens only scanned {curly}; tks.fix_token_format → to_curly_format() converts them) and wrong TOKEN (CANCEL icon — a proper {curly} token not valid for that field; existing tks.strip_invalid_tokens). Generation fallback (core/naming_utils._effective_template() at both generate_name choke points) returns the field's NAMING_DEFAULTS entry when the stored template is invalid, so no literal [scene]/disallowed value leaks into a generated name (Zero-Friction; a self-invalidating per-template cache keeps the hot path off the validity regex; a test guards every default is itself valid so fallback can't loop). One shared NAMING_TEMPLATE_CATEGORIES model (single source, a test guards it covers all 43 TOKENS_PER_TEMPLATE fields) + draw_naming_template_row() (right-aligned label | editable field | conditional red fix buttons | ▾ actions) drive both the prefs Templates tab (was ~140 lines of hardcoded per-category blocks) and the N-panel warning, so the two surfaces are identical.     19. 🟢 The render queue remembers each take's recent render times together with the settings they were measured at. New persisted ViewLayer.tks_render_history StringProperty (panels/context_render_queue.py, HIDDEN, saved in the .blend like the probe estimate): JSON list, newest-first, capped at 3, entries {t: seconds, c: cost proxy at record time, e: engine, ts: unix}. Written ONLY through features/batch_render/shared.py::record_render_actual — FG render_post (render_hooks.py) and both BG done sites (process_manager.py); preview renders are excluded on every path (durations under overridden settings stamped with the real settings' cost would poison the history). Estimates use the cost-rescaled same-engine median (render_queue_eta.history_append/history_entries/estimate_from_history): changing resolution or samples rescales each stored time by the cost ratio instead of trusting it raw or discarding it (with adaptive sampling the stamp is pixels-only — entry Changed 17), cross-engine entries are skipped (a pixels×samples ratio between engines is meaningless), and the median absorbs one outlier run (thermal throttle, background load). Cascade rank 1 in _estimate_vl_render_time, with the legacy session-only tks_last_render_time float as fallback — still written for its other consumers (progress fallbacks, ops_render_queue_resolver). Tests test_render_eta_history.py. Commits cd9935d, 29daade.

    20. 🟢 Value Lock — C4D-inspired locking, rethought as a scene-wide value snap-back, toggled from the nav header. features/value_lock/ package. Semantics (FINAL, user-settled 2026-07-07 — unkeyed-only, the C4D-like lock "only for locking the global changes"): a channel WITH keyframes on the currently assigned action+action_slot is LEFT FULLY UNLOCKED (never snapped, never targeted; a nudged keyed value is re-asserted by the animation system on the next frame change, not by the lock); only UNKEYED channels snap back to their cached lock-time value (a nudged static value silently applies at every frame — the "global change" the lock prevents). engine._keyed_channels(block) is a read-only slot-exact fcurve-membership check (unresolved action_slot = not slot-driven = unkeyed; no cross-slot fallback — that over-detected on same-action VL switches) passed as keyed_now to channels_to_snap. ENFORCEMENT IS SELECTION-SCOPED (f97c970): the feeder schedules only selected/active objects (+ their data/shape keys/materials), so cascade-driven writes on unselected watchlist objects are never fought — log-confirmed root cause of the VL-switch clobbering. An a3c027e experiment (keyed→own-pose snapping via fc.evaluate) was reverted in 89bebb7 per user decision. Snap log: 'snapped N unkeyed value(s), left K keyed channel(s) free'. The feeder's Action-datablock branch was removed (keyed edits are the animator's). Autokey, however, is mutually EXCLUSIVE with the lock (de1d80a): autokey would keyframe every nudge and the unkeyed-only lock leaves keyed channels free, so autokey would let accidental edits exempt themselves. Locking forces autokey off (saving tks_value_lock_autokey_was_on), dims the header autokey button, re-asserts off if re-enabled via Blender's timeline (feeder schedules a pass → engine forces off), and restores on unlock — the v2.1 handling, kept alongside the unkeyed-only engine. Deliberate MANUAL keying still opts a channel out. lock_core.py: bpy-free decision core — capture_paths_for per rotation mode (incl. quaternion/axis-angle), channels_to_snap (EPS idempotency), merge_targets (keyed targets override baseline), prune_dangling, locked_names_in_updates; 20 unit tests in dev/tests/test_value_lock.py. properties.py: .blend-backed store — Scene.tks_value_lock_enabled Bool (flipped ONLY by the toggle operator so flag+capture pair in one undo step), Scene.tks_value_lock_autokey_was_on, and Scene.tks_value_locks CollectionProperty of TKS_ValueLockEntry {id_name, data_path, array_index, baseline}, IDs keyed by NAME string per the PointerProperty ban; lock_all(scene) captures every scene.objects member. engine.py: debounced snap-back (0.1s timer + 0.08s drag-defer, mutation-queue routed, undo/redo + is_snap_suppressed guards). handler.py: read-only depsgraph feeder — cheapest-first enabled gate, autokey-mirror gate skeleton (50ms throttle, Process Monitor "Value Lock", playback/addon_is_mutating/batch skips); reacts to object is_updated_transform hits AND bpy.types.Action datablock updates (covers key deletes turning a channel unkeyed). Rest-state integration: mirror_logic._handle_autokey_mirror and revert_snap._revert_unkeyed_to_rest_deferred stand down while the lock is on (the lock owns the scene — no rest-vs-lock tug-of-war; see doc/troubleshooting/value_lock_cascade_action_fight.md for the v2 cascade-corruption bug this replaced). Autokey integration: engaging the lock remembers autokey and forces it off (a lock prevents keying entirely); unlock restores; the header autokey button dims while locked; feeder+engine force autokey back off if re-enabled mid-lock. operators.py: tks.value_lock_toggle is the single global toggle. UI: the nav-header button between Autokey and Timeline Sync (panels/navigation/panel.py, LOCKED/UNLOCKED + depress) is the SINGLE control (the earlier Inspector status panel was removed). Materials (ce2ff49): the store is generalized to typed (id_type, name) tokens — OBJECT transform channels + MAT node-tree sockets. lock_all also captures every numeric node-socket (inputs AND outputs — Value/RGB nodes hold data on outputs) of every material used by scene objects (add_material_lock, tree-relative nodes["X"].inputs[i].default_value paths that match the tree's fcurve data_paths); resolve_token maps MAT→material.node_tree (values + animation_data owner); the feeder schedules all locked materials on any Material/NodeTree depsgraph update (tree names don't map back to materials cheaply; engine only writes drift); scalar socket writes route through the parent (path_resolve(parts[0]) + setattr). Snap-on-release (ce2ff49): the debounced flush defers while any TRANSFORM_OT_* modal operator is running (Window.modal_operators, verified in 5.1), so the snap happens on mouse release, never mid-grab; slider drags keep deferring via the 0.08s value-change window. Everything-animatable (d07981e + 5532755): capture is now the generic RNA rule — every writable numeric property Blender marks is_animatable (_capture_rna_animatable), over: object props, pose-bone transforms (armatures), modifier RNA props + Geometry Nodes group inputs (ID properties; guarded — most modifier types raise TypeError on .keys()), constraint props, the object's data block, shape-key values, material props, and the scene world (props + node tree). Token kinds grew to OBJECT/DATA/SHAPEKEY/MAT/MATP/WORLD/WORLDNT, each resolving to the block that owns both values and fcurves so the keyed/unkeyed rules apply uniformly; DATA/SHAPEKEY are keyed by the OBJECT name so data renames don't orphan them. The Scene datablock and compositor trees are deliberately excluded — the cascade/render-preset system writes those and the lock must not fight the addon. Engine scales via one-pass grouped_baselines (store holds thousands of entries now) and _write_channel gains int/bool/ID-property write casts. VL-switch + lag fixes (3a2e0fa, corrected by 2d9cdaf): baselines are FROZEN at lock time and never re-based — unkeyed channels always return to their locked value across VL switches, keyed channels follow whatever action is now assigned (fc.evaluate, switch-aware); the only switch handling is a non-sticky stand-down while mutation_queue.is_in_vl_switch_recovery() (new read-only accessor) is open, so enforcement never reads a half-applied action mid-swap. (3a2e0fa first tried re-basing to the arrived-at state via a refresh_baselines poller armed by note_vl_switch; that was racy — it dropped the pending snap and froze an un-snapped user move as the new baseline, and its _awaiting_refresh flag could stick true and silently disable the lock. Removed in 2d9cdaf per user decision.) UI lag killed: the feeder's FOUR full store scans per tick became one cached derived view (token_sets+grouped_baselines, validated by scene/count/enabled, invalidated on refresh and undo-abort). Repro + fix proven by smoke 4i/4j (fails pre-fix). See doc/troubleshooting/value_lock_vl_switch_stale_baseline.md. Known scope: IDs added after locking aren't captured; renamed objects/materials drop out via prune; NLA untouched. Design record doc/roadmap/_dev/value-lock.md. Suite: 865 passed, no new failures; 32/32 live-extension smoke (unkeyed→cached start, keyed→own keyed value, cascade action swap persists untouched, material socket snap unkeyed+keyed, light energy, modifier float, shape key, world background, boolean-cast prop, autokey pause/restore/re-enable guard). Commits 7aa693e, aada3cc, f33792d, 96d030a, c015772, ce2ff49, d07981e, 5532755, 3a2e0fa, 2d9cdaf. VERIFIED in-app 2026-07-08 after a stabilization chain: engine-owned switch clock fed by VL_SWITCH_PRE/POST_CASCADE (f72cfc8+c281e39 — mutation_queue's elastic recovery window is re-marked by preload/slot ops and stretched settling to 20s+), feeder drop-during-1s-settle (chain writes to selected objects must not be enforced), explicit post-switch keyed restore via fc.evaluate writes (frame_set proved a no-op interactively), DRIVEN channels classified animation-owned (25891c7 — snapping a driven value fights the driver forever), and the final root cause of the recurring "same-action switch" reports fixed in the SWITCH PIPELINE itself, not the lock (Fixed entry 17 / ccac6d1).

    23. 🟢 Still & Animation Mode — pin a take's timeline to frame 0. New self-contained feature features/still_mode/ (mirrors rest_state / value_lock); core touched by only a one-line hook. engine.py (context-free, lazy bpy, unit-testable without Blender): clamp_scene(scene, use_frame_set=True) snapshots the scene's real frame_start/end/current + frame_preview_* / use_preview_range into .blend-persisted Scene.tks_still_saved_* props, sets tks_still_active=True, pins frame_start=frame_end=0 (use_preview_range=False) and jumps to 0; restore_scene reverses it verbatim; the tks_still_active guard is the double-capture guard (never re-snapshots the pinned 0→0 over the real range on a Still→Still switch). apply_still_for_vl(scene, view_layer, global_still=None, use_frame_set=True) clamps or restores off the want-rule scene_wants_still(vl, global) = is_still_global() or is_still(vl), so the global master switch and the per-take flag compose automatically (a per-take Still take stays clamped after the global switch goes off). _set_frame uses Scene.frame_set from operator context but a plain frame_current= assignment when use_frame_set=False — the switch-handler path, where frame_set inside depsgraph_update_post recurses/crashes. properties.py: Scene.tks_still_mode on the master scene (global switch, Rest State first-scene pattern), ViewLayer.tks_still (per-take, self-registered like tks_batch_selected), Scene.tks_still_active + tks_still_saved_{start,end,current,preview_start,preview_end,use_preview}. operators.py: tks.still_global_toggle (flips the master flag → apply_still_all_scenes, which re-applies the shared engine to every scene) and tks.still_toggle (scene_name/vl_name args per Rule 71.248, flips vl.tks_still, applies immediately only when the target is the active take of the visible scene). Hook: core/vl_switch.py::_handle_vl_switch_impl calls apply_still_for_vl(scene, view_layer, use_frame_set=False) right after apply_vl_switch_unified, riding the switch's mark_vl_switch_recovery grace window so the saved-range write folds into the switch's own undo step. Render scoping: features/batch_render/batch_pipeline.py::apply_render_overrides (SHARED by the FG modal pipeline AND the headless CLI worker, so one hook covers both) calls apply_still_for_vl(sc, vl, use_frame_set=True) — a Still take renders frame 0, same-scene animation takes restore via the persisted saved frame, and the CLI worker never saves the .blend so the clamp can't leak to the file.     24. 🟢 A Pacing setting (Gentle / Balanced / Fast) chooses how hard the view-layer preloader rests between layer builds. A build occupies the UI thread for its whole duration (a depsgraph build is atomic in Blender — it cannot be sliced or backgrounded), so pacing trades session smoothness against total preload time. New preload_pacing EnumProperty in TKS_AutomationsPropsMixin (default BALANCED), drawn indented under the preload mode for any enabled mode in preferences/draw_workflow.py (prefs-search aware via search_prop/rf); EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 519→520. Pure PACING table in core/vl_preload.py: GENTLE/BALANCED/FAST = rest gap 4×/3×/2× the last build's time, floors 0.5/0.3/0.3 s, caps 5/3/2 s; next_tick_interval(exec, pacing) clamps (unknown tier → FAST). TDD test_next_tick_interval_pacing_tiers. Commit 9bb84f6.

Searching the grid no longer removes non-matching tokens (which reflowed the whole grid on every keystroke) — every token is always laid out and the search only flags a per-cell matched (cell 4-tuple), dimming non-matches in place (trow.active = False) so the layout never moves.     18. 🟢 The batch render ETA now corrects itself while a batch runs. New bpy-free math module panels/render_queue_eta.py (pattern: process_manager_estimate.py), consumed by _get_batch_progress (panels/render_queue_panel.py). Live drift: median actual/estimated ratio over THIS run's DONE takes (collect_drift_ratios/drift_factor, clamped 0.25–4.0; DONE-only — FAILED/CANCELLED durations are truncated) rescales the remaining frozen-snapshot estimates for the ETA text; the bar keeps reading the snapshot so its monotonicity is untouched. Live re-guard (reguard_estimate): a snapshot row disagreeing with the scene's measured reality median by more than STALE_RATIO=2.0 either way — and lacking own measurement — snaps to the sibling median mid-batch (re-guarded rows skip drift; rows with real history are never clamped, so a legitimately-10x hero take survives). Sibling reality via _vl_reality_seconds: session actual OR persisted history — the SKIP_SAVE tks_last_render_time starts every session at 0, which had left the guard blind after each restart. In-flight remainder priority: engine-native Remaining (entry 18) → progress projection elapsed×(1−p)/p blended by p (project_in_flight_remaining; the realness flags TKS_OT_BatchRender._has_real_progress / manager _has_real_progress are authoritative — tks_render_progress also carries the elapsed-based fallback, which would be circular) → estimate − elapsed. Displayed total = recorded actuals for DONE + corrected estimates for the rest. Throttled [BATCH:ETA] diagnostic trace (gated enable_debug_logging + log_topic_batch). FG limitation settled: Blender 5.x render_stats delivers only the final Time:…(Saving:…) string (log-verified + devtalk #220) — no per-sample FG observer exists, so projection is BG-only and the FG Sample X/Y hook stays dormant. Tests test_render_eta_precision.py + test_render_eta_round2.py. Commits c53f5d3, 6c4beca, cd9935d, 29daade.

    19. 🟢 Calibrate Render Times probes each take at a reduced resolution under the real sampling settings. Root cause of the estimate blow-ups: the old worker probed at forced 64²×1-sample / 256²×16-sample points and extrapolated on pixels × nominal samples with a ~100× lever arm — structurally wrong under adaptive sampling (Cycles terminates per pixel at the noise threshold and never nears the nominal cap), and one-off warm-up cost (kernel compile / BVH build) landing in a probe timing multiplied by the lever. Failed intermediate the same day: warm-up + denoise/compositing post-probe + monotonic floor on the two-axis model — reduced the noise but not the structural adaptive error. Final cli_probe_worker.py design (render-farm still-image test strategy rethought for per-VL probing): untimed warm-up, then two probes at 12.5% / 25% of the real output resolution (floor 64px/axis) with samples, adaptive sampling, denoising AND compositing left at scene values; _extrapolate_resolution fits overhead+slope on the pixel axis alone, floored at time_high. Adaptive-aware cost model: use_adaptive_sampling → pixels-only cost in BOTH _vl_cost_proxy and shared.record_render_actual (the two must agree or history rescaling drifts). Probe sanity guard in render_queue_eta.cascade_estimate: a probe disagreeing with the measured sibling median by >2× either way is distrusted → sibling median (still trusted when no sibling reality exists). Fingerprint probe-sharing unchanged. See doc/troubleshooting/render_eta_probe_blowup.md. Commits cd9935d, 29daade.

    20. 🟢 Background batch renders show Cycles' own remaining-time prediction for the in-flight take. Both BG managers parse the engine's Remaining:MM:SS.cc (and HH:MM:SS.cc) field from worker progress lines (process_manager_estimate.parse_remaining_seconds, regex Remaining:(?:(\d+):)?(\d+):(\d{2}(?:\.\d+)?)); _last_remaining/_last_remaining_at on BGRenderManager (+FastBGRenderManager via inheritance), reset per task at start. _get_batch_progress consumes it age-adjusted with a 15s staleness window (engine stops emitting during post) — the engine's estimate is adaptive-sampling- and tile-aware, strictly better than external projection; the sample-fraction projection stays as fallback. Commit 29daade.

    21. 🟢 The VL fast sweep no longer re-verifies slot-token pairs it already stamped — steady-state switch time roughly halved on heavy scenes. Deep post-preload profile (dev/scripts/perf_sweep_deep.py, rig fixture 90 objects / 520 targets / 284 slots) attributed ~50% of the 22 ms steady-state apply_vl_switch_unified sweep to slot_tokens._slot_token_entry: STEP 2 called stamp_pair(target, slot) for every assigned target on every switch, and its get_token(slot) linear-scans the action's tks_internal.slot_tokens RNA collection — O(targets × entries) ≈ 148k RNA reads per switch, superlinear in scene size. Fix in core/vl_switch_fast.py: a token_by_handle = {slot_handle: token} map is built inside the SAME single pass that already builds slot_by_token, and the stamp is skipped when both the target token (cheap RNA read) and the mapped slot token are present — exactly stamp_pair's no-write case, so write behavior is unchanged (missing-side and fresh-pair paths still call it; a successful stamp updates the sweep-local map so same-sweep duplicate binds also skip). Per-target deferred slot_tokens imports hoisted to once per sweep. Safety proof dev/scripts/verify_token_map_safety.py (write-set parity fresh/steady/undo, verdict SAFE_TO_IMPLEMENT); red-first regression guards in dev/tests/test_fast_sweep_tokens.py (steady sweep must do ZERO _slot_token_entry scans + stamp-parity tests). Measured: sweep p50 22.2 → 9.57 ms (−57%), UN/ASSIGN/SNAP identical (520 assigned). Suite 775 passed (the 19 test_preset_dirty fails are the known order-dependent set from 7cd68e6 — all 23 pass standalone). Roadmap notes: doc/roadmap/_dev/perf-hotpaths.md. Commit def4620. ✅ in-app verified.

    30. 🟢 The rest-drift indicator flags keyed-control drift, shows in Rest State Mode, and snaps keyed channels to their own key. get_rest_drifts (features/rest_state/logic.py) previously stood down wholesale in Rest State Mode (added 9917bc8) and only reported UNKEYED channels straying from the Rest Action — so with Value Lock pinning unkeyed values and rest mode suppressing the rest, the ghost drift indicator went dark in every mode the user works in. Rewrote it around one rule: a channel drifts when its live value matches NEITHER the Rest Action's frame-0 value NOR the assigned take's frame-0 key (pure decision _value_matches_any, 12 unit tests). Unkeyed channels — rest is the sole reference (unchanged, valid at any frame). Keyed channels — on-model at their own frame-0 key OR the rest pose; the keyed test runs in Rest State Mode (the flat rest pose holds at every frame) or at frame_current == 0 (off frame 0 a live take pose legitimately differs from frame 0, so keyed channels are skipped to avoid a playback false-positive flood). Because the mode assigns the Rest Action to every ad.action, the real take is recovered via resolve_cascade(CascadeProperty.ACTION, …, raw=True) and matched per target by slot name. Detection classifies drift via the raw take, but the revert DESTINATION follows the CURRENTLY-ASSIGNED action (ad.action — the Rest Action while the mode is on, the take otherwise) at frame 0, rest fallback: shared helper _revert_value(ad, …) feeds both snap_single_to_rest and the drift row's ref_val so the shown value equals the snap. In Rest State Mode a keyed transform (empties, lights) therefore reverts to REST, not the take — the raw resolver had wrongly sent it to the take's key (fixed 5841514); in a normal take a keyed channel still reverts to its own key, an unkeyed one to rest, and keyed-only channels the rest action doesn't cover can be snapped too. Classification helpers _build_raw_take / _take_action_slot / _take_keyed_value. Driver-driven channels are excluded from the scan (_driven_channels via animation_data.drivers, 2b7452e) — their live value is the driver expression, not the raw fcurve, which false-positived against rest (the Li_* light rigs); same exclusion the Value Lock engine makes, and it can't hide real drift. Remaining caveat: constraint / NLA-blend overrides are still unguarded (per-channel heuristics risk suppressing genuine drift; not observed). A per-scan force=True summary logs mode / frame / keyed+unkeyed / driven-excluded counts + example (topic UI·DRAW, gate-bypassing). Tests: test_rest_drift_keyed.py (19 — matches-any, take-resolution, driver-exclusion, revert-fallback) + test_rest_mode.py::test_rest_mode_rest_drift_producer_consults_mode rewritten from the old standdown assertion. Commits f2afddb, a053ebe, 2b7452e, 5841514. ✅ in-app verified.

    40. 🟢 Preloading no longer stutters the viewport between layer builds, and a build waits for about a second of complete stillness instead of firing the moment you pause. Root causes: (1) the rest-gap mini-ticks called signal_redraw() 4×/s from a timer — against its own "never on a timer" contract — tagging whole areas incl. the 3D viewport's WINDOW region → full viewport draw passes all run long (the between-builds lag on heavy scenes). New process_monitor.signal_progress_redraw(include_viewport) tags only VIEW_3D UI (sidebar) regions per pass; the WINDOW region only when the overlay is on (overlay_position != 'OFF'), throttled to 2 Hz in vl_preload._signal_redraw. (2) One still probe (0.25 s) sufficed to build → the freeze landed the instant the user paused; now REQUIRED_STILL_CHECKS = 4 consecutive still probes (~1 s) via pure next_still_count() (any motion resets). The per-layer build freeze itself is Blender physics — a depsgraph build is atomic on the UI thread. Tests test_next_still_count_resets_on_change_and_grows_when_still, test_required_still_checks_is_about_a_second. Commit on fix/preload-idle-redraw.

    50. 🟢 While a take is Still, the timeline scrub bar can't move the playhead — the native playhead lock rides the Still clamp. _apply_playhead_lock (features/still_mode/engine.py) forces scene.lock_frame_selection_to_range = True only for a single-frame clamp (start == end); a defined Animate range and restore_scene hand back the user's own value, snapshotted into the new Scene.tks_still_saved_lock_frame (properties.py) alongside the frame range, so in-place re-clamps (Still ↔ custom Animate range) track it too. Defense-in-depth for Fixed 26 — with the playhead unable to leave [0,0], a scrub on the Still scene can't even start the crash sequence — and it delivers the "inert scrubber" UX (a real gray-out of the native scrub bar has no addon hook).     52. 🟢 Internal: architecture-debt ratchet added to the test suite, with pure/bpy/slow pytest markers — no behavior change. Phase 0 of the decoupling plan (GitHub/.claude/plans/takes-decoupling.md). New dev/tests/test_architecture.py bootstraps the sibling blender-addon-auditor's ARCH-01..05 classifiers over the addon package (locates the auditor by walking up from the test file so worktree runs resolve; skips cleanly when the checkout is absent), applies the frozen grandfather baseline arch_baselines/takes_for_blender.json, and fails on ANY new non-baselined violation. A guard-the-guard test proves the classifiers actually run over the tree (the whole debt surfaces when no baseline is applied), so a green gate means "no new debt", never "the check silently no-oped". pytest markers pure/bpy/slow registered in pytest.ini; the autouse fresh_scene reset is scoped OFF for @pytest.mark.pure tests — opt-out on pure rather than opt-in on bpy, so every existing unmarked bpy test keeps its read_homefile reset — letting plain-Python checks run under bare pytest (pytest -m pure) with no Blender in the interpreter. Commit 8fceea2.

    53. 🟢 Internal: the take-switching core no longer imports panels or features — it announces events and queries the provider registry — no behavior change, fast sweep unregressed. Phase 1 of the decoupling plan, three tranches. (1) Nav-warning + inspector cache flushes became NAV_WARNINGS_INVALIDATE / INSPECTOR_CACHE_INVALIDATE emissions on core/event_bus.py; panels/navigation / panels/inspector self-subscribe invalidate_nav_warnings / mark_inspector_dirty at register time (12 upward core→panels imports removed, all fire-and-forget — commit d7bd6db). (2) The sweep-only post-undo profiler payload is emitted as PROFILER_FEED (navigation subscribes and owns its SWEEP_ONLY_PHASES constant); new core/providers.py — register_provider / get_provider / query / clear, the pull-side inversion companion to event_bus, torn down alongside it — lets the inspector register its _pending_fresh_actions queue as the inspector_fresh_actions capability instead of core importing panel privates (killed an ARCH-01 and an ARCH-03 edge — commit a75650f). (3) The last ~23 core→feature return-value sites inverted onto the registry, each feature registering at enable time: rest_state (get_rest_action, rest_mode_action_name, is_rest_mode, get_rest_drifts, find_slot_collisions, the slot-snap trio, an arm_suppress mirror-suppress setter replacing external pokes at _suppress_until, invalidate_cascade_action_cache, rest-cache ensure/build/invalidate), render_presets (last_applied_preset, is_preset_dirty, find_missing_presets), still_mode (apply_still / apply_switch_snap / reconcile_sync bundle), navigation (get_slot_mismatches, formerly a private cross-package import — commit b5fcd8d). Hot paths (vl_switch_fast, the cascade-clear loop) hoist provider refs into locals once at setup — no query() in any inner loop; every site keeps its original try/except and a matching default so a torn-down / not-yet-loaded feature degrades exactly as the old ImportError skip did. Fast sweep UNREGRESSED: apply_vl_switch_unified clear-all warm p50 2.68 ms / cold p50 5.38 ms (main baseline 2.90 / 5.75; gate 8.98 ms). Seam tests: dev/tests/test_arch_events.py (event constants pure; emit-reproduces-side-effect + provider seam, bpy). Suite 1241 passed / 1 pre-existing skip. ARCH baseline re-frozen 207 → 193 keys (auditor commit 1f3a847) — the ratchet now holds the shrunk debt. ✅ in-app verified (VL switching, cascade, undo/redo, rest & still switches, preset warnings).

    54. 🟢 Internal: cache invalidation routed through a leaf registry — writers stop importing panel draw caches upward — no behavior change. Phase 2 of the decoupling plan. New utils/cache_registry.py (register_cache / unregister_cache / invalidate / invalidate_all / clear): each cache owner registers its invalidator under a topic at register time — navigation "nav_warnings" (invalidate_nav_warnings), inspector "inspector" (mark_inspector_dirty), context panel "vl_cascade" (invalidate_vl_cascade_cache), rest_state "rest_state" (cache.invalidate_all) — and 29 writer sites across 17 files (render_presets ×5 files, rest_state, bookmarks, variant_switch, operators/inspector ×8, operators/cascade ×3, operators/ui ×2, ops_slots_rename, ops_rule_logic, properties/_groups_shared, properties/tag_library, panels/context/properties, panels/inspector ×2) call invalidate("<topic>") on the leaf utils module instead of importing the owning panel upward. Registry semantics: idempotent registration, per-invalidator crash isolation (a broken cache never sinks the writer that announced a change), unknown topic = silent no-op (owner not yet registered → stale-cache degradation, matching the old except ImportError: pass behavior); clear() torn down in core/vl_handlers.py beside event_bus.clear() / providers.clear(). Division of labour vs the bus: event_bus = push notification with semantics, cache_registry = dumb pull-side invalidation fan-out — a writer uses one per concern. Tests: 9 pure registry tests + 4 bpy topic-wiring seam tests + a textual guard that the upward imports never regrow (dev/tests/test_cache_registry.py). Suite from main 1255 passed / 1 pre-existing skip. ARCH baseline re-frozen 193 → 185 keys, 0 new violations (auditor 9f113e2). Freeze gotcha for the record: --arch-freeze-baseline without AUDITOR_SCAN_ROOT scans zero files and writes an EMPTY baseline — always point it at the addon repo. Commit fe40bd4. ✅ in-app verified.

    55. 🟢 Internal: three large code files reorganized into smaller focused modules — no behavior change. (c) ui/styles.py 914→579 — preset_row + preset_selector_row (the ~350-line render-preset widget family) moved to new ui/preset_rows.py and re-exported from styles, so all ~30 styles.preset_row(...) call sites (render_presets panels, cascade level popovers, inspector, globals, channels) are untouched; ui/__init__ imports the new module. Also utils/manual_map.py now opens with a GENERATED DATA — DO NOT SPLIT/MOVE header (the MANUAL_MAP table is auto-written by dev/scripts/apply_wire_assignments.py, one row per wired control; it must stay in the shipped package because register() hooks bpy.utils.register_manual_map).
