    56. 🟢 Camera Visibility Automation caches the per-scene camera list instead of scanning scene.objects every switch. apply_camera_visibility (core/cascade.py) scanned all of scene.objects on every VL switch to find cameras, so switches slowed as a file accumulated cameras/objects — only with the automation on. New per-scene cache _camera_vis_cache = {scene_name: (object_count, (camera_name, …))}; the O(objects) scan reruns only when len(scene.objects) changed or a cached name no longer resolves to an in-scene camera (add / remove / rename / unlink — a same-count swap is still caught by the name check), otherwise the cached list is reused (O(cameras)). Invalidation policy is a pure, RED-first unit-tested core core/camera_vis_cache.py::camera_cache_valid (5 tests, dev/tests/test_camera_vis_cache.py). The cache lives behind the auto_camera_visibility early-return so the feature-off path stays zero-cost; names only, never object refs (stale-pointer ban). Also surfaced in the switch profiler (Added 26) so the fired/skip state + time are observable. Confirmed working in-app with the automation on. Troubleshooting doc/troubleshooting/camera_visibility_switch_slowdown.md. Commit 1047563.

    Fixed¶

    1. 🟢 Clearing all keyframes at the current frame now affects only the scene you're working in. PERF-03 review of the 12 bpy.data.objects for-loops surfaced one genuine over-reach: the keyframe-clear operator's use_all_targets branch (operators/inspector/ops_keyframes.py) built its global targets from context.scene (scene + scene.world + node trees) but then iterated bpy.data.objects for the per-object targets — so a "remove all keys at current frame" wiped keys on objects in every scene, inconsistent with its own scene-scoped Scene/World targets. Scoped the object walk to scene.objects. Strictly narrows the blast radius (can only clear ≤ what it did before); aligns the object scope with the already-scene-scoped global targets.

    2. 🟢 The View-Layer Preload panel no longer gets stuck open after a preload finishes. The nav-bar toggle renders only while _preload_show = is_preloading() or cold_count() > 0 (panels/navigation/panel.py), but the panel BODY drew on tks_show_preload_panel alone — so when a run completed (not preloading, 0 cold) the toggle vanished while the body kept drawing, stranding it open. Two-part fix: (a) the body draw is now gated on the same is_preloading() or cold_count() > 0 condition, so it auto-hides when there's nothing to show; (b) at natural queue-drain completion in core/vl_preload.py::_preload_tick, if cold_count() == 0, reset wm.tks_show_preload_panel = False so next time a layer goes cold the (red) badge re-appears closed rather than the panel silently re-opening. The toggle's update callback no-ops on a False write (and tks_show_preload_panel isn't self-mutually-exclusive on turn-off). See doc/troubleshooting/preload_panel_stuck_open.md.

    3. 🟢 A view layer visited by an interactive switch reverted to COLD in the preload panel. _preloaded_this_session had only two writers — reset_preload_state() and _preload_tick — and the tick excludes the active layer (pair == active_pair → continue). So nothing recorded a layer preloaded by switching, and the layer switched away from fell through ACTIVE→PRELOADED→PENDING to COLD despite its depsgraph still being cached. Fix: new vl_preload.mark_preloaded(scene, vl) (idempotent), called from core/vl_switch_fast.py::apply_vl_switch_unified — the single sweep every path funnels through (interactive / load-apply / batch / preloader), always for the layer being built. Deferred import (vl_preload imports vl_switch_fast → top-level would be circular). The load-apply records the initial active layer; each switch records the to-layer; the active-first check keeps the current layer showing ACTIVE. Tests: test_mark_preloaded_* in dev/tests/test_vl_preload.py. See doc/troubleshooting/preload_visited_layer_shows_cold.md.

    4. 🟢 The public roadmap is now a live board that keeps itself up to date, with a clearer layout. Source of truth stays in doc/roadmap/{ideas,active,done} (status = folder; _dev/ private). dev/scripts/build_wiki_roadmap.py rewritten: emits three Markdown tables (Feature · Meta · What) + per-feature pages; parse_meta now also reads the required **Size:** token; board_table collapses Theme/Area/Size into one Meta column of Material icons with { title= } tooltips, the feature title is the page link (no Link column), the size dot is :material-circle:{ .sz-* }; wrap_phases wraps ## Phases in a .phases div so CSS marks non-task <li> with an ⓘ glyph; board_blurb trims summaries; intro admonitions dropped; new --addon-root so the wiki CI runs it against the cloned .addon-src. .github/workflows/notify-wiki.yml now also triggers on doc/roadmap/** + the generator. doc/ROADMAP.md demoted to a pointer; every feature file gained a **Size:** token; doc/roadmap/README.md, the roadmap skill, and the global Auto-Push rule updated to the one-push flow (chose Option A — generate-in-CI — over moving the human source into the wiki).

    5. 🟢 VL-switch rest-snap silently skipped objects whose rest slots changed since the cache was built. apply_vl_switch_unified STEP 3 read get_cached_rest_values() behind only a lazy if _rest_cache is None guard; invalidate_rest_cache() is called only on rest-keyframe write/revert, so when the Rest Action's slot set changed any other way (e.g. snapshotting newly-selected objects) the cache stayed incomplete and those objects fell out of ref_by_slot → SNAP=0. A full Blender restart rebuilt the cache and masked it (diagnosis: pre-restart sweeps all SNAP=0; post-restart KEY_HITS=94, SNAP 2–28). Fix in features/rest_state/cache.py: new ensure_rest_cache_fresh() + pure _rest_cache_needs_rebuild(cache_present, live_names, cached_names) rebuild when the live Rest Action slot-name set diverges from _rest_slot_targets (add/remove/rename), not only when None; shared _slot_cache_name() helper (hoisted _ID_PREFIXES). core/vl_switch_fast.py calls it in place of the lazy build. See doc/troubleshooting/vl_switch_same_action_keyed_snap.md.

    6. 🟢 Same-action VL switch reset animated objects (notably Empties) to their Rest values. STEP 3's keyed-path exclusion matched the Rest action slot name against a keyed_paths set keyed by the cascade action slot name. Those names diverge for Empties — the Rest slot is {object} (ctrl_drawer_S_03) but STEP 2 renames the cascade slot to the template label {object}_EMPTY (ctrl_drawer_S_03_EMPTY) — so the keyed location path was not excluded and got snapped to rest; on a same-action switch the depsgraph never re-evaluates, so the bad snap stuck (laser trace: chosen_key='ctrl_drawer_S_03', name_in_ref=True label_in_ref=False, location[2] live=0.38379931 ref=0.37821015 willsnap=True, then stuck at the rest value). The manual path (get_rest_drifts/snap_single_to_rest) was always correct because it reads keyed paths from the target's actual assigned slot fcurves (identity). Fix in core/vl_switch_fast.py: build keyed_by_handle = {slot_handle: {(data_path, array_index)}} from the cascade action during the slot pre-scan; new pure helper keyed_paths_for_assigned_slot(keyed_by_handle, ad, target_action) matches by slot handle (rename/template-proof); STEP 3 skips those paths. Duplicate-slot theory ruled out (chosen_key and ref values were correct/stable). Tests: dev/tests/test_vl_switch_rest_snap.py (11 — handle exclusion incl. the Empty name-mismatch case + cache-freshness add/remove/rename); 152 adjacent rest/VL/slot tests still pass. See doc/troubleshooting/vl_switch_same_action_keyed_snap.md.

    7. 🟢 Naming-template rows in Preferences showed a doubled dropdown chevron. Each row's ▾ actions popover (draw_naming_template_row in preferences/draw_naming.py) is layout.popover(panel_id, text="", icon='DOWNARROW_HLT'). In the Preferences/Add-ons editor Blender draws a popover button's own native disclosure chevron whenever the button has spare width, so the explicit DOWNARROW_HLT icon (dim, left) and the native chevron (bright, right) both rendered — width-gated (it vanished as the window shrank and the button lost slack). The Properties editor (Smart Output popovers) doesn't add the extra chevron, so the byte-identical call is single there: an editor-surface behaviour, not the popover call/panel/layout. Ruled out (all confirmed not the cause): the compact scale_y on Slots-Object-Data, removing the icon (→ bare wide chevron), dropping align=True from the label/field split, changing the generated panels' bl_space_type/bl_region_type to 'PROPERTIES'/'HEADER' (user: "no change"), and restructuring to the Smart-Output flat-row layout (still doubled). Fix: pin the ▾ to a fixed icon-width cell so the editor can't give it spare width — pop = input_row.row(align=True); pop.ui_units_x = 0.8; pop.popover(...) — single clean ▾ at any window width. Diagnosed with a throwaway GUI-Blender screenshot probe (open real prefs → maximize → screenshot → zoom the button column), since the bug is invisible to headless tests. See doc/troubleshooting/naming_template_popover_double_chevron.md.

    8. 🟢 The File Name preview now resolves even when the Directory is invalid; a bad directory no longer collapses the Output panel. Root cause: the directory preview's else branch (taken only when the directory is valid) did a LOCAL from ..smart_syntax.engine import SmartSyntaxEngine, which makes the name local to the whole draw_output_panel_prepend function. When the directory was invalid that else was skipped, the local was never assigned, and the File Name preview's later use of SmartSyntaxEngine raised UnboundLocalError: cannot access local variable 'SmartSyntaxEngine' → its try/except fell back to the raw, unresolved pattern ([view_layer]_####.[file_format]). Invisible headless (the bug is in panel-draw scope, not the resolver). Fix: drop the shadowing local imports (it's already imported at module scope). Found only via a diagnostic that surfaced the caught exception text in the preview. Several real but non-causal defensive fixes were made along the way (each made the failure degrade more gently, which is why the symptom kept moving): resolve_token/resolve_path now except Exception per-token (a cluster raising a non-(RuntimeError, AttributeError, KeyError) type no longer bubbles out and blanks the whole path — degrades just that token to [token]); the #### frame pass prefers the PASSED scene over bpy.context.scene and is guarded separately so a frame error can't discard token resolution; .alert moved from the directory preview box() to an inner row() (setting alert on a box() corrupted draw state and silently dropped the next box — the File Name preview); and the Output override wraps the prepend in try/except so a bad path can't drop the native Saving/image-settings section. Commits 07e66ea (the fix), ef32b48, dda7952, e99ddcf, 785bd5c. See doc/troubleshooting/smart_output_invalid_dir_filename_unbound.md. ✅ in-app verified.

    9. 🟢 Reset / Clear actions in the Build Syntax popover repaint the field, chips and preview immediately. Clicking Reset / Clear Last / Clear All changed wm.tks_token_builder but the keep-open popup only updated after a mouse move — Blender doesn't auto-redraw a floating keep-open popup when a child popover closes. The Clear and Reset operators now tag every editor for redraw so the popup repaints instantly (the final real Menu form also closes cleanly, repainting on close). Commit 8c43622. ✅ in-app verified.

    10. 🟢 Right-click → Online Manual reaches a feature page for ~100 more controls (INFO-04 wiki manual-map). Hand-wired the newer / namespaced operators and renamed redo-panel fields the AUTO-WIRED category pass in utils/manual_map.py misses, so the auditor's INFO-04 manual-map coverage dropped from 101 elements falling back to the wiki home to 4. New hand-maintained MANUAL_MAP entries (placed after the AUTO-WIRED block, before the safety-net catch-alls; lowercase, win-first) route: token builder + field_* → features/smart_output/; *output_rule* / rule-override → features/rules/; rq_* / render-queue / stat_info / detect_render_version / toggle_render_path_mode → features/batch_render/; pm_* / monitor-switch / profiler → features/process_monitor/; dm_* → preferences/debug/; tab/toggle_*_panel toggles + tree-design → interface/navigation_panel/; *tag_filter* → features/tags/; smart_undo/smart_redo → interface/hotkeys/; *action_name + toggle_autokey → interface/inspector_panel/; pies/keyframes → features/pie_menus/; toggle_version_warning → features/vl_versions/; *preload* / vl-settings copy-paste → interface/context_properties/; toggle_globals_mode → features/globals/; rebuild_cache → preferences/advanced/; plus per-class redo-field patterns for the renamed rest_state ops (snappropertytorest, unsetrestkeychannel, deleterestslot) the stale AUTO-WIRED *reference* entries no longer match. The four generic UI-list controls (tks.list_add/remove/move/clear) intentionally stay on the wiki home — reusable plumbing with no single page to document. Verified by replaying Blender's lowercase fnmatchcase matcher: 97 of 101 reroute, 0 uncovered, no test_manual_map.py contract violation.

    11. 🟢 The Take Name naming template kept reverting to an invalid value on fresh starts after a headless test-suite run (prefs autosave leak). Tests in dev/tests/test_token_builder.py pointed the Token Builder's WM target at the REAL naming_take_template pref; the live write-through (features/smart_syntax/properties.py::_builder_to_target) pushed fixtures (junk{scene} → [sep][hostname] → [scene][sep][take], last write wins) into AddonPreferences, and update=_autosave_preferences full-dumped the config over the developer's real user_preferences.json. Every GUI start then loaded the poisoned template (register-time load_saved_preferences() overrides both the property default and userpref.blend), the naming warning fired, and quit re-saved the value into userpref.blend — an in-app fix held only until the next test run. Fix: TKS_TEST_MODE env kill-switch in _autosave_preferences() (env var, not a flag — mid-suite addon_enable reloads prefs and would re-arm a Python flag), set by dev/tests/run_tests.py; snapshot/restore in the two prefs-targeting tests; syntax tests pin tks_token_target_kind='none'; new regression test dev/tests/test_prefs_autosave_guard.py asserts a pref write leaves the config byte-identical. Both stores repaired (JSON + headless save_userpref()). Commit 7cd68e6. See doc/troubleshooting/take_template_test_prefs_leak.md. ✅ in-app verified.

    12. 🟢 Calibrating render times no longer produces multi-minute estimates for takes that actually render in seconds. User-reported: 2 of 7 takes (~10s real render) showed ~22-minute estimates after Calibrate; the header ETA summed to ~24m. Three stacked root causes: (1) structural — the old probe extrapolated on pixels × nominal samples, which is ~100× wrong under Cycles adaptive sampling (see Changed 17 for the resolution-only probe redesign); (2) guard blindness — the probe sanity check read sibling reality from the session-only SKIP_SAVE tks_last_render_time, which is empty right after every restart, so stored garbage probes passed unchecked into the per-row labels AND the frozen batch snapshot (fixed by history-backed _vl_reality_seconds + the mid-batch reguard_estimate rescue, Changed 16); (3) verification blocked — a full day of in-app checks silently ran stale code because the Blender 5.1 extension junction pointed at the paused custom-tokens worktree (%APPDATA%…\extensions\user_default\takes_for_blender → .worktrees\Takes-for-Blender-custom-tokens); repointed to the main checkout — always verify the junction target before an in-app session. See doc/troubleshooting/render_eta_probe_blowup.md. Commits cd9935d, 29daade. ✅ in-app verified.

    13. 🟢 A background preload no longer overwrites camera, world, or action choices you made by hand. The restore leg re-applied the active layer's cascade resolution (_apply_preload_cascade(saved…)), not the actual prior state — manual deviations were stomped once per tick, and a layer resolving no camera CLEARED scene.camera (core/cascade.py None-branch, ~:548) / scene.world under auto-clear (~:635). core/vl_preload.py now captures a names-only raw snapshot per touched scene on first touch (_capture_scene_snapshot: camera/world/compositing_node_group/use_nodes + per-target (action.name, slot.identifier) keyed (obj.name, label) via iter_anim_targets) and the restore leg writes it back verbatim with guarded writes (pure restore_writes — equal values write nothing ⇒ nothing dirtied ⇒ restore-leg evaluated_depsgraph_get() dropped; target-leg eval kept — it IS the preload). Active snapshot recaptures when the user switches pairs mid-run (snapshot_needs_recapture). Names-only invariant enforced by non_name_values (no ID refs — PointerProperty-ban analog). start_preload also swapped the stale _rest_cache is None guard for ensure_rest_cache_fresh() (from 2ed1c31) so preload can't bake an incomplete rest cache. 7 TDD pure-helper tests in dev/tests/test_vl_preload.py. See doc/roadmap/_dev/preload-viewport-integrity.md. Commit e30b9d9.
    14. 🟢 Scenes shown in a second window are no longer switched around by a background preload. Only the user's scene+layer was restored; other scenes kept the last-preloaded VL's camera/world/compositor/actions. Every touched scene is now snapshot-captured on first touch and guarded-restored every tick (_restore_scene_snapshot(target_scene) first, then the active scene so shared objects end on the active layer's assignments); cancel / process-disable / batch-interrupt / addon-disable paths run _restore_all_snapshots(). Commit e30b9d9.
    15. 🟢 The VL Switch Profiler now repaints fully on an undo/redo re-fire (was single-writer + stale header + blank skipped groups). The profiler tree (wm.tks_profiler_items) had exactly one writer — the switch operator's deferred cascade in operators/context/ops_crud_switch.py — so the post-undo re-fire (core/vl_lifecycle.py::_maybe_refire_cascade_snap), which runs apply_vl_switch_unified directly and discarded its (_perf, _stat), left the panel showing the previous operator switch. Three stacked fixes: (1) extracted the ~90-line inline tree build into panels/navigation/profiler_feed.py::rebuild_profiler_tree(wm, perf, sweep_perf, sweep_stat, target_action_name, rest_action_name, ran) — ran (OPERATOR_PHASES vs SWEEP_ONLY_PHASES) marks phases the caller didn't execute as SKIPPED; the operator calls it with full groups (byte-parity), the re-fire with sweep-only (WM props aren't undo-tracked, so the deferred-timer write can't desync the undo stack — same pattern as the tks_cascade_step_* icons the sweep already sets there). (2) The header reads full_ms = tks_cascade_time_total + tks_cascade_time_eval, but tks_cascade_time_eval was written only by the operator, so a sweep-only rebuild left the prior switch's (dominant) eval time frozen; the helper now owns that prop (from perf['blender_eval'], 0.0 when absent) and the re-fire measures + times view_layer.update() when the profiler/cascade-steps panel is open (opt-in, safe in the deferred timer — the warm-up timer evals there too). Redraw switched to signal_redraw_deferred() because the profiler is a template_list and a synchronous tag_redraw from a timer skips the list's layout re-eval until a mouse move. (3) A SKIPPED group header rendered its timing cell blank (_draw_group only printed a time for exec_ms >= 0), reading as "not calculated"; extracted panels/navigation/monitors_profiler.py::group_timing_display(exec_ms, status) → dimmed "skipped" label + greyed header. Re-running overrides/finalize on undo is intentionally NOT done — apply_overrides() mutates materials/objects and fights Blender's native undo restore — so skipped is the correct state, now legible. Tests: dev/tests/test_profiler_feed.py (8), dev/tests/test_profiler_display.py (3), all red-first. Commits 821f266, 2b6569b, 0d92ea5.     17. 🟢 Same-action VL switch left a nudged keyed object at the nudge. Root cause (user-pinpointed via the Watchlist pipeline: "the snap is not firing between the same actions"): the fast sweep's STEP 2 writes ad.action = target_action only when the action CHANGES; that assignment write is what tags the target for animation re-evaluation, so a same-action switch performed no write, no re-eval happened, and a user-nudged keyed channel kept its nudge (different-action switches restore as a side effect of the write). STEP 3's rest snap can't cover it: it excludes every path the cascade action animates — and when the cascade action IS the rest action, that excludes everything. Fix: in the sweep's no-write branch, target.update_tag(refresh={'TIME'}) forces the same re-evaluation an action change causes; sweep summary log gains RETAG=N. Mechanism verified headless; confirmed in-app 2026-07-08. Works with the Value Lock off too. core/vl_switch_fast.py, commit ccac6d1. See doc/troubleshooting/vl_switch_same_action_no_reeval.md.

    19. 🟢 Deleting/unlinking the Rest State action while the mode is on now AUTO-EXITS cleanly (mode off, autokey + Value Lock restored, button grays); exiting the mode always restores both. Two-part follow-up to Added 21, with a UX revision superseding an interim red click-to-exit button (commit fd93fc3) via user-chosen auto-exit. (1) Auto-exit reconciler. No crash was ever possible — get_rest_action() is bpy.data.actions.get(name) (None on delete) and every rest read is None-guarded — but the mode went "zombie": flag on, autokey paused, resolver falling through to the real tree action. A deletion is first observed in draw / property-update contexts (mutation ban), so the fix is a one-shot timer: schedule_orphan_reconcile() (idempotent, gated on rest_mode_broken()) registers _reconcile_orphaned_rest_mode, which runs in a safe context and calls the shared deactivate_rest_mode(context, restore_lock=True) — set_rest_mode(False) + restore_autokey + _reapply_active_vl (reassigns the real tree actions) + Value-Lock restore. The reconciler defers (returns 0.15) while TKS_VL_STATE.addon_is_mutating/is_undoing/is_redoing, never throws into the timer loop, and is unregistered on addon unregister. Scheduled from two sites: the toggle's poll (per-redraw) on a mode-on orphan, and _on_rest_action_update (properties.py) for popover unlink/change. TKS_OT_RestModeToggle.poll now grays whenever not has_rest_action() (mode on OR off) — the prior "keep enabled to exit when broken" is obsolete since the reconciler auto-exits; the interim red alert= row and dynamic description() broken branch were removed. deactivate_rest_mode writes state DIRECTLY (not via the now-grayed toggle) so the auto-exit can't be blocked by its own poll. (2) Symmetric Value-Lock restore (unchanged from fd93fc3): entering sets Scene.tks_rest_mode_lock_was_on before releasing the lock; exit re-enables it after restore_autokey + reapply; recursion avoided via restore_lock: BoolProperty(default=True, SKIP_SAVE) (the Value-Lock reverse exclusion passes restore_lock=False). Ordering: restore_autokey (→ ON) then re-enable lock (→ re-pauses) reproduces the pre-mode state. Tests: test_rest_mode.py (pure — poll grays-always truth table, orphan-poll schedules reconcile, schedule idempotency + orphan-only, deactivate/schedule wiring, restore_lock+memory, reverse restore_lock=False) and test_rest_mode_sweep.py (registered end-to-end, @_needs_followup now also gates on deactivate_rest_mode: auto-exit-on-delete via the shared helper + lock round-trip). Junction serves MAIN → registered tests validate post-merge. Design record doc/roadmap/_dev/rest-state-mode.md. Worktree full suite 1027 passed / 0 failed; post-merge registered gate 3/3. Commits fd93fc3, f59a319.
    20. 🟢 A background preload no longer leaks another take's action onto your current take when you click an object afterwards.     21. 🟢 While a preload run is live, working in the viewport no longer stutters between layer builds, and a stray action can no longer land on your current take mid-run.     26. 🟢 Dragging the timeline playhead while a Still take was active hard-crashed Blender (EXCEPTION_ACCESS_VIOLATION @0x28). Root cause (source-confirmed in the 5.1 release branch): Screen.is_animation_playing is a GLOBAL getter over ED_screen_animation_playing, which counts screen->scrubbing — so a Timeline drag reads as "playback" with NO animtimer. The Still auto-stop then ran screen.animation_cancel, and 5.1's stop_playback() (screen_ops.cc) reads screen->animtimer->customdata — wmTimer.customdata sits at struct offset 0x28, the exact faulting address — with no null guard, so the op segfaulted even under the probe-proven temp_override(window, screen) (guarded upstream after 5.1). Three production crashes: 2026-07-10 19:43 (Eloise), 2026-07-12 00:10 + 08:38 (Basketballkorb). This CORRECTS the 2026-07-10 red-herring verdict — the playhead drag was never incidental; scrubbing is an independent, sufficient trigger. Fix (features/still_mode/handlers.py): _scrub_somewhere() (per-screen is_scrubbing across ALL windows — the C-side acts on the FIRST playing-or-scrubbing screen) consulted by the frame_change scheduler AND re-checked inside _stop_still_playback (a scrub can begin between scheduling and firing); _scrub_end_watch (0.1 s poll) snaps Still playheads home with plain frame_current writes once the scrub ends; both timers cleaned up in unregister_handlers. TDD: 2 predicate tests + a source-contract regression lock in dev/tests/test_still_mode.py; RED observed pre-implementation; suite 1212/0 post-merge. See doc/troubleshooting/still_mode_playback_cancel_crash.md (updated with the scrub mechanism). Commit 87297e5.

    Removed¶

    1. 🟢 The Preferences → Workflow → Naming → Tokens sub-tab (token reference browser) removed — build syntax now lives only in the shared Build Syntax mega-sheet. Deleted the active_subtab_naming == 'TOKENS' branch in preferences/draw_naming.py along with the Templates/Tokens sub-tab nav row — the Naming tab now draws templates directly (no sub-tabs). Trimmed the file's now-dead imports (draw_info_box, draw_indented_column, draw_accordion_chevron, draw_subsection_gap; PREFS_NAV_SCALE_Y, PREFS_TITLE_SCALE_Y, PREFS_TITLE_GAP, ICON_EXPAND_OPEN/CLOSED). Removed the orphaned prefs and their traces: naming_token_filter EnumProperty (props/props_naming.py, plus its PROP_ADDONPREFERENCES_NAMING_TOKEN_FILTER import and the tooltip constant in texts/tooltips_preferences.py), active_subtab_naming EnumProperty (props/props_navigation.py), and the 14 expand_tokens_* BoolProps (props/props_logging.py); purged them from persistence_io.UI_STATE_KEYS and the addon_prefs_constants.ACCORDION_GROUPS "Naming > Tokens" tuple; dropped the naming_token_filter special-case in draw_data_inspector (the data-driven NAMING_TOKENS inspector bucket stays — it still holds use_smart_output*). Kept tks.copy_token / get_token_descriptions (preferences/naming.py) — a generic clipboard op the Token Favorites roadmap (doc/roadmap/_dev/token-favorites.md) builds on; still wiki-mapped in utils/manual_map.py. The one survivor with no other editor, naming_separator, was relocated rather than dropped (see Changed entry 6) — net EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 496→481 (−16 here, +1 there). The mega-sheet token model (token_builder.categorized_tokens, the Smart Output popover, the node panel) is untouched. Headless suite green (617 passed, 1 skipped); ✅ in-app verified.

    2. 🟢 The naming-template unlock gate removed — every template is editable directly. Removed the naming_templates_unlocked BoolProperty (props/props_naming.py; its bpy.props import slimmed to StringProperty only, since BoolProperty/EnumProperty were now unused) and the entire lock card + unlock toggle in preferences/draw_naming.py::draw_naming_tab. The temporary LOCKED/FREE category split (added the same session) was collapsed back into the single NAMING_TEMPLATE_CATEGORIES list (original order), which the tab now draws unconditionally; the orphaned 'naming_templates_unlocked' key was dropped from the draw_data_inspector session-state key filter. EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 481→480. Rationale (verified at the source): naming templates are generators, not matchers — bindings are identity-based, so changing a template only affects newly created names and can never break an existing connection: cascade datablocks (actions/cameras/compositors, Rest Action) are tracked by name + UUID self-heal (bpy.data.<coll>.get(name) + tks_*_uuid repair), and action slots are paired to their targets by a UUID token (core/slot_tokens.py ensure_token/get_token, stored on the target and on the owning Action keyed by slot handle). detect_slot_renames compares a slot's name_display to the template's expected label only to offer a cosmetic rename — never to bind. So the unlock gate guarded nothing. ✅ in-app verified.

    [0.7.10] - 2026-06-24¶

    Added¶

    1. 🟢 Absolute/relative path mode for the Smart Output directory — one-shot convert + A/R field badge. New features/batch_render/path_mode.py (pure logic + thin operator, mirrors token_builder.py). Pure: path_mode(s) (RELATIVE/ABSOLUTE/NEITHER by leading prefix only), is_absolute, to_absolute(s, blend_dir), to_relative(s, blend_dir). Whole-string conversion — tokens ([scene], ####) are inert path text and survive because only the ///drive prefix is rewritten, so no path↔token splitting is needed. to_relative normalizes os.path.relpath returning '.' (the .blend's own folder) to '', so blend-dir → // not //.; returns None on a Windows cross-drive ValueError. Operator tks.toggle_render_path_mode (REGISTER/UNDO/INTERNAL): reads scene.tks_render_directory, flips it via the pure fns using dirname(bpy.data.filepath), signal_redraw(); reports {'WARNING'} (clear wording) on unsaved file or cross-drive; state-aware description(). Registered after token_builder in batch_render/__init__. UI in panel.py: draw_output_panel_prepend badges the Directory field with EVENT_A (absolute) / EVENT_R (relative) glyphs set as the field's own prop(..., icon=…) — the house pattern from preferences/draw_data_storage.py::_draw_storage (plain prop when empty); TKS_PT_DirPatternActions adds a contextual Make Absolute/Relative item with the same letters. Tests: dev/tests/test_path_mode.py (14 — classification, conversion, cross-drive None, token survival, //↔abs round-trip incl. the //. regression, icon-enum validity, operator registered) + test_row_action_menu.py updated for the new contextual item. Repro-driven debugging (the real trigger was an unsaved .blend; // can't resolve without a save anchor) documented in doc/troubleshooting/path_mode_toggle_double_slash.md. A follow-up fix added path_mode._canonical() (applied in path_mode/to_absolute/to_relative) so a single leading \\ is read as the Blender-relative // — mirroring the renderer's exact rule in properties._get_expected_filepath — instead of as an absolute UNC path, which had made the badge disagree with what actually rendered. Full suite 475 passed headless. Follow-up: TKS_OT_ToggleRenderPathMode gained a poll() returning False when not bpy.data.filepath with cls.poll_message_set("Save the .blend first — '//' relative paths anchor to its location"), so the popover's Make Absolute/Relative item is grayed (with a reason) on an unsaved file instead of relying on the execute-time {'WARNING'} cancel.

    2. 🟢 Token Builder popover for Smart Output naming patterns — click-to-build with live search and chips/field editing. New features/batch_render/token_builder.py: pure logic (parse_segments / join_segments / move_segment / remove_segment / append_token / match_token / format_token_for / tokens_for_filter, headless-tested in dev/tests/test_token_builder.py, 28 tests) + thin INTERNAL operators (tks.token_builder_append / _select / _move / _remove / _clear / _copy / _apply) + volatile WindowManager state (tks_token_builder / _search / _filter_kind / _filter_key / _target_kind / _target_data / _bracket_mode / _title / _sel_idx / _edit_mode, all SKIP_SAVE). Launcher-Op (ui_patterns Rule 54): ops_smart_output.TKS_OT_SyntaxCheatSheetPopover.invoke seeds the WM state (Seed+Replace via _read_target) and opens a keep-open, button-less popup with wm.call_panel('INVOKE_DEFAULT', name="TKS_PT_TokenBuilderPopup", keep_open=True) — chosen over invoke_props_dialog (forces OK/Cancel) and invoke_popup (closes on the first operator click). panel.py: TKS_PT_TokenBuilderPopup INSTANCED panel; draw_smart_syntax_cheat_sheet dispatches to _draw_builder_columns (popover — draw_builder_strip + a uniform grid_flow(columns=4, even_columns=True, even_rows=True) token grid with flat emboss=False/alignment='LEFT' items; search filters at 3+ chars) vs _draw_cheatsheet_accordion (docked sidebar, copy-on-click). tks_token_edit_mode EnumProperty {CHIPS, MANUAL} switches between movable-chip and raw-field views of the same pattern. Registered after properties in batch_render/__init__; launched from the Directory / File Name popovers' Build Pattern item.

    3. Layout pass (draw_builder_strip): content wrapped in a padded inner column (outer = layout.box(); top/left/right/bottom separator insets) so controls don't crowd the border; the live search box moved to the bottom of the box (function-body level, after the if/else) so it sits in both Chips and Manual modes just above the grid it filters; mode editor and search each get a separator(factor=1.2) lead gap.     4. Edge graying + pinned // root: new pure has_pinned_prefix(segments) (leading literal starting with //). move_segment rejects any swap touching index 0 while pinned; move_segment_to_edge won't move the root and lands a far-left relocate at index 1 (after the root). Draw grays the left pair when sel==0/sel==1-behind-a-pin and the right pair on the pinned root, so the // chip is locked far-left and nothing slides in front of it — moving it would yield an invalid mid-path //. +8 headless tests in test_token_builder.py (53 total in-file).

    6. 🟢 Fixed path-navigation tokens // and ../ — verbatim inserts, treated like the fixed separators. New core/naming_utils.FIXED_PATHS (single source, re-exported by engine): {literal: (label, tooltip)} for // ("Relative root") and ../ ("Up one folder"). Inserted VERBATIM (not bracketed) so the renderer, the abs/rel badge, the Make Relative/Absolute toggle, and the far-left pin keep reading the literal leading // — a bracketed [//] would break all four.     7. 🟢 View-Layer Preload — the first switch to each take no longer stalls. New core/vl_preload.py. Pure, bpy-free decision core (tested in dev/tests/test_vl_preload.py): build_preload_queue (order-preserving, excludes active + already-preloaded, generic over (scene,vl) tuples), mode gating should_auto_preload/should_show_button/preload_enabled, preload_eta_seconds/_fmt_eta, iter_preload_states/cold_count/pair_state, section_key/is_section_collapsed/toggle_section/scope_pairs. Engine: a per-tick safe_register timer preloads ONE (scene, view_layer) pair across ALL scenes — saves window.scene+view_layer, activates the target with the cascade depsgraph handler suppressed via TKS_VL_STATE.is_applying, runs the FULL cascade (_apply_preload_cascade: resolve_cascade(ACTION) + apply_overrides(skip_action=True) + apply_vl_switch_unified(..., rest_action=None) — rest_action=None disables the snap so no transforms move, but the with-action depsgraph eval is built), forces evaluated_depsgraph_get(), then restores the active layer; mark_vl_switch_recovery() + drain() fold it off the undo stack (net-neutral data). start_preload() pre-builds the global rest cache (features/rest_state/cache.build_rest_cache, read-only) so the first real switch doesn't pay that one-time build (the residual "rest delay"). AUTO fires from vl_lifecycle._deferred_load_apply; reset_preload_state() on load. Process "VL Preloader" (TIMER/CORE, expected_interval=0 → IDLE, never auto-restarted). Nav UI: WindowManager.tks_show_preload_panel (accordion callback) → red badge in panels/navigation/panel.py (gated preload_enabled + is_preloading or cold_count>0); sub-panel panels/navigation/warnings/preload_viewlayers.py::draw_preload_panel walks wm.tks_all_viewlayers with a layout-container STACK to nest collapsible SCENE_GROUP/SCENE/VL_GROUP boxes (independent collapse in _preload_collapsed), with layout.progress(type='BAR'), ETA, value_box per-layer state chip, and a tks.preload_viewlayers.section_key Preload at every level (additive start_preload(scope)). Operators tks.preload_viewlayers / tks.cancel_preload_viewlayers / tks.preload_toggle_section (ops_crud_switch.py). The residual delay was diagnosed with a temporary ctx.view_layer.update() probe in _deferred_cascade → it's Blender depsgraph eval (cold ~1600 ms → preloaded ~110 ms → revisit ~50 ms), inherent to single-valued shared action assignment (preload holds every VL's topology but only the active VL's animated state). Full history in doc/roadmap/_dev/vl-preload.md. Suite 548 passed.

In _output_panel_draw_override, the reproduced native rd.filepath row was previously always drawn with filepath_row.enabled = not smart_on (grayed when Smart Output on); it's now gated if not smart_on: so it isn't drawn at all while Smart Output owns the output — the resolved Directory/File Name previews above already convey the final path, and a disabled duplicate was pure clutter. The use_property_split = False/use_property_decorate = False setup moved inside that guard. Added a layout.separator() at the end of draw_output_panel_prepend for spacing between the file-name preview box and the native Saving/image-settings section. No tests (pure draw-layout change in the panel override).

    32. 🟢 Shift+Click a group chevron to expand or collapse a whole list at once. Converted 5 execute-only collapse-toggle operators to the invoke→shift_all = event.shift→execute pattern (mirrors pm_toggle_group_expand), each gaining shift_all: BoolProperty(default=False, options={'HIDDEN'}): tks.profiler_toggle_group (every GROUP_HEADER in tks_profiler_items), tks.preload_toggle_section (new vl_preload.set_all_sections_collapsed, computing section keys from wm.tks_all_viewlayers), tks.vsw_tree_toggle (every tks_vsw_tree item), tks.tagtree_toggle_expand (every tks_tree_expand_<cat> WM bool, enumerated from lib.categories), tks.tag_group_toggle_expand (every group.is_expanded across all categories). Shift state = inverse of the clicked item applied to all; plain click unchanged. Audit of all collapsible lists found these 5 missing it (Takes tree toggle_scene_expand and Process Monitor pm_toggle_group_expand already had it).

    Fixed¶

    1. 🟢 find_vl_version_set() re-resolves the set by collection index to stop a stale-RNA EXCEPTION_ACCESS_VIOLATION (@0x18). The helper cached live TKS_VLVersionSet element references in a module global, invalidated only by a length-token + rename event. Heavy custom-property churn on the World reallocates the IDProperty array backing tks_vl_version_sets without changing the element count, so the token never fired and a dangling element was returned — the next draw's len(vs.versions) dereferenced a freed IDProperty group and hard-crashed. The id_data guard can't catch it (the World ID stays alive, only the element slot moved). Fix: cache the collection INDEX and re-resolve sets[idx] from the freshly-fetched collection every call, with an identity re-check that rebuilds on a silent reorder; prefer the scene_name StringProperty over the .scene PointerProperty (Constitution Rule 1). draw_vl() wraps len(vs.versions) in try/except as defense in depth.

    2. 🟢 Pie-menu toggle update= callbacks return None. navigation_pie_enabled and f12_pie_menu_enabled used update= lambdas that returned a TUPLE of two calls (autosave + keymap sync). Blender requires update callbacks to return None, so registration raised ValueError: the return value must be None and the headless test runner crashed (exit 2, 0 tests). Replaced with named functions that call both and return None implicitly.

    3. 🟢 Autokey-mirror suppression was writing _suppress_until to the wrong module in two VL-switch call sites. core/vl_switch_fast.py:56-57 (in apply_vl_switch_unified, "Suppress autokey mirror handler" block) and operators/context/ops_crud_switch.py:162-164 (in TKS_OT_SwitchViewLayer._deferred_cascade) both imported features.rest_state.operators as _ref_ops and wrote _ref_ops._suppress_until = time.time() + N. The flag is defined and read from features.rest_state.mirror_logic (mirror_logic.py:29, checked at :48); writing it to operators silently creates a transient attribute on the wrong module that _handle_autokey_mirror never reads. Effect: both suppression windows were dead — the handler could fire during Action reassignment and produce double rest-state captures or unexpected snaps on VL switch. Pre-existing in both sites; not introduced by the module split. Correct write sites (cascade_actions.py:137, cache.py:321, logic.py:312,511) all use mirror_logic as _ml; _ml._suppress_until = ... correctly. Fix: changed both imports to mirror_logic as _ml; companion stale comment at vl_lifecycle.py:495 corrected ("Suppress was removed — _suppress_until is dead code" was false; only vl_lifecycle's own write was removed, the mechanism is live).

    4. 🟢 Sync Brackets now normalizes mismatched delimiter pairs (e.g. [scene)), not just whole-style differences. New SmartSyntaxEngine.convert_to_current_style(path) replaces the per-style conversion loop: a single module-level regex _ANY_BRACKET_TOKEN = re.compile(r'[\[{<(%$#]([^\[\]{}<>()%$#]+)[\]}>)%$#]') matches any-open + any-close (matched or not), and a _repl that rewrites to the current get_brackets() pair only when the inner is a known token (KNOWN_TOKENS or a _PARAMETERIZED_TOKENS base after :-split) — so arbitrary bracketed text, native #### padding (no inner content), and unknown tokens are untouched (Rule 71.437). needs_bracket_sync(path) = convert_to_current_style(path) != path, draw-safe (never raises), drives the conditional red button (Changed #9). ops_utils.TKS_OT_SyncBrackets.execute refactored to call convert_to_current_style (dropping its inline per-style loop + BRACKET_STYLES import), so detection and repair share one implementation. [scene)/(scene]/{scene> → [scene] (current style); verified by hand-traced cases + headless compile.

    5. 🟢 to_absolute normalizes ../ segments (was leaving literal .. in the field). features/batch_render/path_mode.py::to_absolute now wraps os.path.join(blend_dir, tail) in os.path.normpath(...) (then .replace('\\','/')), so .. collapses against the .blend folder — //../../[scene] from C:/proj/shots → C:/[scene]. Anchored at the file root (blend_dir = dirname(bpy.data.filepath)); tokens are ordinary path components and survive. to_relative already normalized via relpath, so the abs↔rel round-trip is stable. +2 tests (test_to_absolute_collapses_parent_segments, test_parent_segments_round_trip); 18 path_mode tests pass. Documented in doc/troubleshooting/path_mode_toggle_double_slash.md (3rd follow-up).

    6. 🟢 A Rest Action whose backing action was deleted now loads showing the name in red, not blank. The file-load handler only copied the saved Rest Action name into wm.tks_rest_action when the action datablock still existed, so a rest action deleted and then saved reloaded blank instead of red. Dropped the existence gate — the name is restored regardless, letting the popover render a missing action as red/stale, matching the runtime behaviour where deleting a live action shows the field red, not empty. (Files saved while already blank stay blank until the action is re-picked and saved — nothing was persisted to restore.) Added TestRestoreHandlerKeepsStaleName; full headless suite 518 passed. Commit 7daa5b4.

    7. 🟢 The Context tree view now repopulates on every file open, not just the first in a session. The tree stayed blank after the second-plus File ▸ Open: the sync timer's fast-path gate is driven by module-level globals that survive a file load, but the WindowManager-backed tree collection is reset by Load UI — so with nothing to re-arm the gate, sync_all_viewlayers was skipped on every load after the first. Added a persistent load_post handler (twin of the existing undo/redo handler) that re-arms the dirty flags, clears the fingerprint + structure key, and busts the UIList caches so the next timer tick rebuilds the tree. Verified in-app; 543 headless tests pass. Commit f712876.

    8. 🟢 The VL Switch Profiler's categories collapse, and stay collapsed. Two defects. (1) TKS_UL_Profiler (panels/navigation/monitors_profiler.py) had no filter_items, so tks.profiler_toggle_group flipped a GROUP_HEADER's is_expanded (and the chevron) but template_list still drew every child row — added filter_items delegating to a pure collapse_filter_flags(items, bitflag) that clears the filter bit on child rows of collapsed groups (tested in dev/tests/test_profiler_collapse.py). (2) ops_crud_switch._deferred_cascade rebuilds tks_profiler_items on every VL switch (items.clear() + re-add), and fresh GROUP_HEADERs defaulted is_expanded=True → every switch re-expanded all categories; now captures the collapsed group names before clear() and sets g.is_expanded = name not in _collapsed_groups on rebuild. Companion: new generic auditor rule CORR-10 (in the separate blender-addon-auditor repo) flags any UIList drawing a collapse chevron with no filter_items; # CORR-10-OK sentinel added to TKS_UL_ProcessMonitor, which legitimately rebuilds its collection each draw.

    9. 🟢 Editing a view layer that uses the Rest Action no longer snaps your changes back. The autokey-mirror handler's mirror phase already bows out when authoring the rest VL (mirror_logic.py, cascade_action == rest_action → continue, ~L387), but the two revert scheduling sites did not, so _revert_unkeyed_to_rest_deferred (revert_snap.py) reverted the just-edited, unkeyed property to the Rest Action's fc.evaluate(0) (the OLD baseline) ~0.1s later. Clearest with autokey OFF: a transform drag on the rest VL collected the object's action (= the rest action) into _revert_names → schedule_revert({rest_action}) → snap-back — and the rest action's own FCurves were never changed by an autokey-off drag, so the revert read the stale frame-0 value. Fix: new pure predicate revert_snap.revert_names_for_rest_vl(modified_names, rest_action_name, cascade_action_name) drops the rest action from the revert set only when cascade_action == rest_action, wired into both mirror_logic.py sites (the autokey-off branch and the post-mirror has_action_update branch) via _get_vl_cascade_action(context). Take actions modified in the same tick still revert; a normal VL is untouched (the autokey-off snap-to-rest behavior is preserved). Rejected the broader "skip every rest-action target inside the deferred timer" approach — pinned objects on a normal VL legitimately keep sub-targets in the Rest Action (mirror_logic.py ~L382), and the precise "are we on the rest VL?" signal is only reliable at the live-context schedule site. 7 new pure tests (dev/tests/test_rest_vl_revert.py) + 60 rest tests pass headless. doc/troubleshooting/rest_vl_revert_snapback.md.

    10. 🟢 Auditor CORR-07 (Missing poll()) cleared on the 8 flagged operators — quality 9.6 → 10.0. The 0.4 quality deduction was entirely missing_poll_real (8 × 0.05). Each got a poll() mirroring its existing draw-time .enabled gate (no new behavior beyond also guarding direct/keymap invocation): features/batch_render/token_builder.py — TKS_OT_BuilderMove/TKS_OT_BuilderRemove → wm.tks_token_sel_idx >= 0 (matches btns.enabled = has_sel), TKS_OT_BuilderCopy → non-empty wm.tks_token_builder, TKS_OT_BuilderApply → wm.tks_token_target_kind != 'none' (matches apply_row.enabled); all getattr-guarded against a missing WM. TKS_OT_BuilderAppend annotated # POLL_NOT_NEEDED (appending is unconditional; the auditor reads the marker in the two lines above the class def). features/rest_state/operators.py — TKS_OT_SnapAllToRest/TKS_OT_SnapPropertyToRest → get_rest_action() is not None (same cheap module-global lookup the sibling Unset*/Delete* ops already poll on). operators/context/ops_crud_switch.py — TKS_OT_PreloadViewLayersCancel → vl_preload.is_preloading() (lazy import, returns the _preloading module global). Confirmed no direct bpy.ops.tks.* call sites for these idnames (only utils/manual_map.py string entries), so the new polls can't surface as execute-time poll failures. Re-scan: missing_poll_real 8 → 0, harmless 294 → 295 (Append moved to the marker bucket), quality/footprint/health all 10.0.

    11. 🟢 Auditor STD-01 (Manifest validity) cleared — blender_manifest.toml license gains the SPDX: prefix. license = ["GPL-3.0-or-later"] → ["SPDX:GPL-3.0-or-later"]. Blender's local extension validator is lenient, but extensions.blender.org rejects the bare identifier; the SPDX-prefixed form is what the platform requires. No change to the license terms.

    [0.7.9] - 2026-06-05¶

    Added¶

    1. 🔴 Preset-JSON compatibility gate + Clean Up (migrate/quarantine). New features/render_presets/serialization/compat.py (bpy-free except a light from ....core.constants import ADDON_VERSION): validate_preset_data(preset_type, data) → (ok, reason) checking (a) structure — ≥1 non-_meta group with a properties dict; (b) _meta.schema_version int ≤ CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION (a DEDICATED format version, decoupled from the addon version — coupling them would falsely flag presets from any newer build; _meta.addon_version from ADDON_VERSION is stamped as provenance only and never gates); (c) _meta.preset_type match. migrate_preset_data upgrades the one known old format (bookmark export list {"type":"tks_bookmarks","bookmarks":[…]} → preset dict). serialization/crud.py: save_preset stamps schema_version+addon_version+preset_type; load_preset validates → skips incompatible (logs, falls through to next tier); list_presets returns compatible-only via mtime-cached _file_compatible (hot path — called per-type/per-redraw); added list_incompatible_presets and non-destructive quarantine_preset (→ _quarantine/ subdir, never deletes). ops_compat.py (NEW, registered in the feature __init__): TKS_OT_CleanupIncompatiblePresets (scan-all → migrate-or-quarantine behind a blast-radius invoke_props_dialog). Surfaced: nav badge only when incompatible presets exist (tks_show_incompatible_presets + _incompatible_cache in panels/navigation/panel.py, draw_incompatible_presets in warnings.py, registered in panels/navigation/__init__.py); ui/styles.py::preset_row distinguishes INCOMPATIBLE (file exists but fails validation → find_preset_tier not None while absent from compatible list_presets) from MISSING, routing to the cleanup op. Tests dev/tests/test_preset_compat.py (21). Doc doc/troubleshooting/preset_json_compatibility_and_capture_coverage.md.
    2. 🔴 "Check Coverage" preset-capture diagnostic. serialization/resolve.py gains a zero-overhead module _COVERAGE_SINK (None by default; when set to a list, _capture_properties_from_struct records every writable prop it can't store — path/RNA-type/reason). ops_compat.TKS_OT_PresetCaptureReport runs a capture of all types via preset_engine._capture_for_type with the sink and fills WindowManager.tks_capture_coverage (TKS_CaptureCoverageItem PG + TKS_UL_CaptureCoverage), drawn as a template_list in preferences/draw_data_storage.py (no console output, mirroring the Property Scanner). Surfaces the known drops: collection properties + ENUM_FLAG round-trips.

Both collectors consume it: _get_inspector_keyed_paths merges the normalized driver/NLA paths into the displayed set with a {path: source} tag map, and _get_key_count_for_target adds them to the current-frame total so the nav/type badge count matches the displayed list (the CORR-09.1 count-vs-list contract). An NLA-only object (active animation_data.action empty after an NLA push-down) now stays selectable in the type header instead of dropping to "No animated data". Closes the drivers + NLA-only strips entries from CORR-09's overseen-surface inventory; the CORR-09 Tier-2 probe (dev/scripts/channel_coverage_probe.py, dev/tests/test_channel_coverage_probe.py) proved the gap. Tests dev/tests/test_channels_driver_nla.py (3: source-tag surfacing, drivers don't inflate the keyed set, NLA-only object stays selectable).

    4. 🟢 Choose what happens to a duplicated object's animation — Strip / Independent Slot / Off. New auto_duplicate_action_mode pref on AutomationsPropsMixin (EXPECTED_PROP_COUNT 493→494). When an object is duplicated it inherits the source's slot token, creating two live targets for one slot; detect_slot_renames now skips shared tokens (a shared_tokens set) so the rename pass doesn't flip name_display nondeterministically between the two objects. New core/slot_split.py + TKS_OT_SplitDuplicateSlot (operators/inspector/ops_split_duplicate_slot.py) give each copy its own canonical slot in the correct action; core/slot_tokens.py and the inspector viewport-sync updated in step. Commits ac457d9, 33e885a, 284b14d.

    Changed¶

    4. (c) Reference-state mirror logic (features/rest_state/mirror_logic.py, −570).     6. 🟢 The Debug Monitor opens large log files faster. New _read_tail_lines() seeks from EOF and doubles the read window until it captures the requested line count, reaches the file start, or hits an 8 MB ceiling — so load time scales with lines displayed, not the whole (potentially multi-MB) log. Extracted _parse_lines() so the parse + level-filter step is reusable without loading duplicate data. Tests: dev/tests/test_log_reader_tail.py. Commit d3e2ad6.

    Fixed¶

    1. 🟢 Pie "Reset to default" buttons now work. All five slot-reset operators (TKS_OT_ResetPieOptions, TKS_OT_ResetF12PieOptions, TKS_OT_ResetKeyframePieOptions, TKS_OT_ResetKeyframeAltPieOptions, TKS_OT_ResetPieGrid) used prefs.property_unset(slot), which reverts the value in data but emits no RNA update notification → stale Preferences dropdowns and no update=/autosave (the reset was lost on reload). Replaced with two shared helpers in preferences/persistence_io.py (re-exported from persistence.py): reset_pref_slots_to_default(p, slot_names) — setattr(p, key, prop_rna.default) (same path as TKS_OT_ResetPreferences) inside prefs_loading_guard(), then one _autosave_preferences(), then redraw_preferences_areas(); and redraw_preferences_areas() — tags open PREFERENCES areas (the no-direct-tag_redraw rule covers the 3D viewport, not the Preferences window, which signal_redraw() can't reach). Call sites: preferences/ops_misc.py, panels/pie_menus/keyframe.py, panels/pie_menus/render_scope.py. See doc/troubleshooting/pie_reset_to_default_no_effect.md.

    2. 🟢 Switching between view layers with no action reliably snaps objects back to the rest pose — including right after you edit the reference. Two root causes from the v0.7.x single-sweep refactor. (a) Write/read slot divergence: insert_rest_keyframe deposited ref values via Blender's slot auto-match (ad.action_slot after assigning the action), which drifts to a stray duplicate object slot (Name_001_MESH) when one exists, while the snap reads the canonical name_display slot — so a set reference and the snap targeted different slots. Now insert_rest_keyframe prefers the caller-resolved canonical slot over auto-match. (b) Stale ref cache: the frame-0 ref-value cache (features/rest_state/cache.py::_rest_cache) was invalidated only by insert_rest_keyframe, so authoring the reference via native Auto-Key on the reference VL (which writes the FCurves directly) left the cache stale and action-less VLs snapped to the old pose. mirror_logic._revert_unkeyed_to_rest_deferred now calls invalidate_rest_cache() when the rest action is among the modified actions. Failed approaches (reverted): guarding resolve_cascade to return None for the rest action broke the watchlist ghost icon (draw_layers.py derives is_ref from resolve_cascade); and refusing to assign/merge the rest action (apply_vl_switch_unified demote-to-None, merge_action_into_cascade refusal) broke authoring on the reference VL — that VL is the intended authoring surface, so the reference must remain assignable/mergeable. The reference must resolve normally; only the write/read slot consistency and cache freshness needed fixing. See doc/troubleshooting/rest_state_duplicate_slot_write_read_divergence.md. Tests: dev/tests/test_rest_state.py::TestInsertRefKeyframeSlotTargeting, ::TestReferenceModificationInvalidatesCache.

    3. 🟢 The watchlist's VL-switch progress icons reflect actual work. apply_vl_switch_unified blanket-set all six wm.tks_cascade_step_* enums to SUCCESS at the end of every sweep — and because the interactive switch calls apply_overrides(skip_action=True), the accurate per-step tracking in cascade.py (reset→PENDING, then mark each phase) was skipped. The sweep now resets all six to PENDING at the start and, at the end, marks resolve/targets/done SUCCESS (always-run phases) but unassign/assign/snap SUCCESS only when _stat shows they did work — so the inspector icons (panels/inspector/inspector_sections.py: active = step=='SUCCESS', alert = step=='FAILED') read bright=fired / dimmed=not-fired. ("Red on crash" not yet wired.) Test: dev/tests/test_rest_state.py::TestCascadeStepIndicatorsReflectWork.

    4. 🟢 Bookmark presets show a change-warning + Save/Revert. preset_state.get_preset_state routes 'bookmark' to a membership-aware _bookmarks_state (dynamic key set — symmetric add/remove/relabel diff) BEFORE the fixed-schema if not preset_props/_auto_upgrade_preset path; bookmark mutations call _invalidate_bookmark_dirty_state (features/bookmarks/operators.py → invalidate_preset_cache('bookmark') + invalidate_nav_warnings() + signal_redraw()). 'bookmark' added to the Save-All loop / _TYPES / Revert-All lists (+ capture/apply branches) and to both TKS_OT_SelectPreset attr_maps (X-clear + Alt+X-delete were silent no-ops). See doc/troubleshooting/bookmark_preset_no_change_warning.md. (Note: an empty assigned bookmark preset short-circuiting to CLEAN is a known remaining edge — separate.)

    5. 🟢 Bookmarked channels visible without keyframes — rows AND category buttons. (a) panels/channels/logic.py::_get_inspector_keyed_paths merged bookmarked paths RAW (double-quoted, with the node_tree./data. accessor prefix) into active_paths, while active_paths/keyed_paths/section props use the normalized form (normalize_rna_path → single quotes, prefix stripped) — so an unkeyed bookmarked node/material property never matched a section prop. Added _normalize_path_for_type(path, selected_type) (same per-type strip + normalize_rna_path as the keyed loop) applied to each bookmarked path, building a NEW set so it doesn't alias keyed_paths. (b) panels/channels/draw.py::draw_channels filtered the per-target category buttons to keyframe count > 0, so a bookmarked-but-unkeyed target was dropped → "No animated data" + no buttons; now a target is kept when it has keys OR (tks_show_bookmarks and get_bookmarked_paths(scene, target_type) non-empty). Test dev/tests/test_bookmark_channel_visibility.py (RED proved the raw-vs-normalized mismatch); doc bookmark_channels_visible_without_keyframes.md.

    6. 🔴 Material / World / File-Output no longer silently dropped by preset dispatch. ops_manage_sync.py: material branch added to _type_to_attr + _capture_for_save + _apply_to_scene (per-type Accept&Sync of a material preset returned None → "Could not capture settings" CANCEL / getattr(config, None) failure). ops_manage_crud.py::TKS_OT_EditRenderPreset: the rename scene-config if/elif chain (dropped fileoutput/material/bookmark) replaced with a generic _ATTR_MAP lookup, and material added to the tag-ref attr_name map (bookmark stays out — TKS_Tag has no bookmark_preset field — marked # CORR-08-OK). preset_health.py: bookmark added to preset_types + _TYPE_LABELS (a stale config.bookmark_preset is now flagged). panels/navigation/panel.py:170: world added to the nav dirty-scan tuple. All surfaced by CORR-08 (below). Tests dev/tests/test_preset_dispatch_bugfixes.py; doc preset_type_dispatch_material_bookmark_gaps.md.

    7. 🟢 The Inspector channel search filters live as you type. WindowManager.tks_channel_search (panels/inspector/__init__.py) is consumed at DRAW time by panels/channels/{draw,sections}.py (search_term = getattr(wm, "tks_channel_search", "").lower()), but the prop had no update= callback and no options, so Blender only committed the typed value — and redrew — on Enter/focus-loss (text buttons don't write the RNA value mid-edit). Added options={'TEXTEDIT_UPDATE'} (the one StringProperty flag that fires update= on every keystroke during text editing) plus a redraw-only callback _on_channel_search_changed that calls signal_redraw() (Constitution Rule 3 — not tag_redraw()) and is guarded by the addon_is_mutating/is_undoing early-out. Deliberately does NOT call mark_inspector_dirty() (unlike _on_filter_changed): the channels view filters at draw time, so the heavier full-collection resync on the 0.2s sync timer is unnecessary per keystroke. Doc doc/troubleshooting/channel_search_live_filter.md. (The objects-list filter tks_inspector_filter retains its Enter-only commit — same TEXTEDIT_UPDATE fix applies if wanted, but it routes through mark_inspector_dirty().)

    8. 🔴 Orphaned transient .NNN reference baseline slots from action-duplication splitting now reliably swept. core/slot_split.py: the post-split cleanup of baseline slots the ref-state had baselined under a copy's transient .NNN name replaced a single mutation_queue.enqueue_mutation(_clean_transient_ref_baselines, scene.name) pass with _enqueue_ref_clean(scene.name) — a bounded, deduped retry chain. A baseline only becomes orphaned once its object is renamed away from .NNN, so the one-shot sweep raced the copies' auto-rename and left some behind; the retry chain re-enqueues until they've all settled.

    9. 🔴 Project presets resolve to the same folder at startup and after a reload. _get_project_presets_dir now owns the blend-dir/presets fallback as its single source of truth (read via getattr to avoid _RestrictData during addon registration), so register and the deferred reload resolve the same path. Commit 108cf6d.

    Tooling¶

    Maintainer-only — the doc/reports/ /stats code-quality dashboard. Not shipped in the add-on zip; no takes_for_blender/ runtime change.

    1. Overview layout gains a committed factory baseline plus Export / Import of the custom state. The hardcoded DEFAULT_OVERVIEW_LAYOUT in js/app.js is now only a fallback (_FACTORY_FALLBACK_LAYOUT); the real factory baseline lives in the new committed data/dashboard_layout.factory.js (window.DASHBOARD_LAYOUT_FACTORY), loaded via a <script> sidecar before app.js (same cache-buster pattern as codebase_stats.js) and resolved in app.js with a missing-file fallback. Three new sidebar controls: Reset to factory (_resetToFactory — removes only the live tks-overview-layout.v2 key and re-renders from the sidecar; leaves the tks-overview-layout-saved.v2 Save snapshot intact), Export layout (_exportLayout — Blob download dashboard_layout.json wrapped {schema_version, exported_at, layout}), and Import layout (_importLayout — hidden <input type=file> → JSON.parse → accepts the wrapped or a bare layout → existing _migrateLayout reconciliation → save + re-render, with console.warn + label-flash on bad input). download / upload icons added to the ICONS dict; inline feedback via a small _flashLabel helper (mirrors the Save button — the viewer has no toast). The page is static file://, so a download/upload is the only file channel.

    2. Settings popover reorganized into nested fly-out submenus. The flat ~10-button popover is grouped into Data / View / Layout / Tiles categories (.settings-group → .settings-cat row + .settings-submenu). Submenus are position: fixed, positioned to the right of the category from its bounding rect with a viewport-bottom clamp; open on hover and toggle on click, with a 200 ms close-timer bridging the category→fly-out gap, and close together with the popover (Esc / outside-click / resize). All existing button ids/classes are preserved, so every handler and the shared popover-button CSS still apply (.settings-cat added to those selector lists; collapse rule broadened to .settings-popover button > span).

    3. Per-tile show/hide with empty-section collapse. Hidden tile ids live in the layout object (layout.hidden), so visibility travels with Export / Import, resets with Reset-to-factory, and is captured by Save / Restore; _migrateLayout carries the list forward filtered to live data-tile-ids. New Tiles fly-out (_buildTilesMenu, rebuilt on open) lists every tile by data-tile-label with an eye toggle (_setTileHidden / _getHiddenTiles) plus Show all / Hide all; eye_off icon added. _renderOverviewLayout skips hidden tiles — they stay in the already-hidden #overview-tile-pool, keeping their grid slot — and tags columns/sections with zero visible tiles .is-empty. CSS hides .is-empty only via body:not(.layout-mode), so empties collapse in normal view but stay visible as drop targets in layout-edit mode (no re-render needed on mode toggle, since _setLayoutMode toggles the body class).

    4. New audit rule CORR-09 — Channel Coverage / Animatable-Value Routing (Tier 1, static). Catches the "this animated value never shows up in the Channels panel" class. The panel (panels/channels/) buckets each animated data_path into a UI type via substring path_filter lambdas; values are silently dropped three ways, each now checked statically by engine/parts/corr_09_channel_coverage.py::classify_part_channel_coverage (AST-only — the channel modules import bpy, so the part reads logic.py/draw.py from disk via ast.parse, exactly like CORR-08 reads _ATTR_MAP; degrades to channel_present=False when absent). 09.1 routing drift: the two collectors in panels/channels/logic.py — _get_inspector_keyed_paths (drives the displayed list) and _get_key_count_for_target (drives the badge count) — must encode the SAME per-type container set, else the badge and the list diverge. Container tokens are harvested ONLY from path_filter bindings (lambda body, or a local def assigned to path_filter like the ps_filter pattern), so the per-bone selection filter (bone_filter, applied directly to all_fcurves, never bound to path_filter) and the path-normalization block — both legitimately display-only — don't register as drift. Normalization via _norm_container (pathy [/trailing-. tokens + a bare-word vocab: shape_keys/key_blocks/nodes/…); BoolOp(And) branch tests (selected_type == "DATA" and obj:) and in (...) sets both narrow the type. 09.2 type symmetry: the UI type universe is the *type_info list literals in panels/channels/draw.py (tks.select_inspector_target rows); every UI type must be branched by the display resolver (unhandled → empty panel) and every branched type must be a real UI type (orphan → dead branch). 09.3 canonical surface diff: a maintainer-curated _ANIMATABLE_SURFACES inventory (mirrors CORR-03's seed symbol table) tags each animatable ID surface with the covering UI type or None; a None (or a covered_by the UI doesn't expose) is an "overseen" surface — currently 6: scene compositor node tree, grease-pencil layers, NLA-only strips, drivers, non-active materials, Freestyle line style. Sentinel # CORR-09-OK: <reason> on/above a type's branch in either collector exempts that type's drift (reuses crash_06's _s_line_has_sentinel). Scoring (report.py): 09.1 drift + 09.2 unhandled/orphan deduct 0.3 each from quality (functional band, == CORR-08 functional + Part CA); 09.3 surfaces deduct at CHANNEL_SURFACE_DEDUCT = 0.0 (informational-until-reviewed, mirroring COMPAT_DEDUCT_PER_FINDING) so landing the rule surfaces the gap list without re-baselining the health score. Wired into rules.py (CORR-09, CORR/HIGH/quality), state.py (channel_* metrics), report.py (import + dispatch after CORR-08, penalty pen_channel, quality-deduction summary row, full markdown ## Part CORR-09 section, dashboard summary + detailed CORR-09 part JSON). Current real-codebase result: 0 drift, 0 symmetry gaps, 6 overseen surfaces (score unchanged at 7.6). Tests: dev/tests/test_channel_coverage.py (29, incl. the keystone test_real_channel_files_present_and_collectors_agree guarding the shipped collectors against future desync).

    5. CORR-09 Tier 2 — headless ground-truth channel-coverage probe. The static Tier-1 check can only diff against a maintainer-curated surface list; Tier 2 proves the gaps against REAL Blender data. dev/scripts/channel_coverage_probe.py (run headless via tests_perf.py::run_channel_coverage, scraped between ===CHAN_JSON_BEGIN/END=== sentinels exactly like perf_capture.py; behind a --no-channel CLI flag, stored in m.channel_probe) builds a controlled scene that animates representative values across surfaces AND animation sources — action_slot (the only source routing reads), driver (obj.driver_add), nla_strip (rotation authored then pushed to an NLA track with the active action cleared), non_active_material (2nd material slot, distinct metallic path so no collision masks it), and compositor (scene.compositing_node_group, the Blender 5.x global compositor — legacy scene.node_tree is gone) — then drives the LIVE _get_inspector_keyed_paths for every selectable type, unions the surfaced (normalized) paths, and classifies each animated value as surfaced or fall-through. Pure aggregation in dev/scripts/channel_coverage_core.py (classify_coverage / normalize_path — no bpy, unit-tested directly). Each builder is defensive: an API mismatch is recorded in builders_failed (no silent caps), never sinks the run. Current probe result: 9 animated values, 5 surfaced, 4 fall-through (driver scale, NLA-only rotation_euler, non-active-material metallic, compositor nodes["Viewer"].location), 0 regressions, 0 unexpected-surfaced — empirically confirming the four structural gaps the static list claims. Scoring: only probe regressions (a curated-covered surface the live routing FAILED to surface) deduct (0.3 each, folded into pen_channel); the expected-overseen fall-throughs are informational (they confirm known gaps). Report: a ### Tier 2 block in the ## Part CORR-09 markdown + probe payload on the dashboard CORR-09 part. Tests: dev/tests/test_channel_coverage_probe.py — the pure core (9 cases incl. quote-normalization collision matching + regression/unexpected detection) plus test_probe_runs_and_confirms_structural_gaps, an in-Blender integration test asserting driver/NLA/non-active-material fall through and zero regressions.

    6. New audit rule CORR-08 — Preset-Type Dispatch Exhaustiveness (Tier 1, static). engine/parts/corr_08_preset_dispatch.py AST-extracts _ATTR_MAP from preset_state.py (the canonical 9 preset types, read from disk like CORR-09 — the module imports bpy) and AUTO-DETECTS any literal (dict keys / flat token seq / enum (id,…) tuples) already containing ≥75% of the canonical types as bare tokens, flagging the missing ones — no in-code opt-in marker (that first design was rejected by the maintainer); intentional subsets opt out with # CORR-08-OK (and attribute-name lists like _PRESET_FIELDS, which store *_preset names not bare tokens, are never candidates). Findings carry an impact tier (functional 0.3 / cosmetic 0.05) and an informational same-name "sibling-drift" signal (e.g. two type_info maps that disagree). Wired into rules.py (CORR-08, CORR/HIGH/quality, sentinel CORR-08-OK), state.py (preset_* metrics), report.py (penalty pen_part_preset, quality-row, ## Part CORR-08 markdown, dashboard summary + detailed JSON). Also: the dashboard side-menu now spells out category names (rules.py::CATEGORY_NAMES → taxonomy name → js/app.js, with CATEGORY_FULL_NAMES fallback). Tests dev/tests/test_preset_dispatch_exhaustiveness.py — the check surfaced 19 real gaps; the functional ones (material/world) are fixed in Fixed #6, the architectural subsets exempted with CORR-08-OK.

    7. New audit rule INFO-05 — Naming Conformance (informational, no deduction). engine/parts/info_05_naming.py::classify_part_naming replays doc/standards/naming_conventions.md over the AST — 7 sub-checks (NAME-01..07): file names (§2 folder patterns + forbidden / stdlib-shadow), registered class names (§3 TKS_<infix>_<Pascal>, base-branched + acronym / feature-infix aware), operator idnames (§4.1 tks.<snake>), custom-property infixes (§4.2 _PROP_INFIX_ALLOW ~70 tokens — static from bpy_props_registered / prefs_props_registered, plus a dynamic setattr(owner, f'tks_…', …Property()) JoinedStr/Constant re-walk where mid-token interpolation right after tks_ → naming_unverifiable, never flagged), feature↔directory agreement (§6 _FEATURE_REGISTRY ∃-containment; cascade scope-tier prefixes exempt; verb-first idnames never mistaken for codes), uppercase class sub-namespace infix (§3 — only VSW/PIE registered), and ASCII / byte limits (§5: idname ≤60, class ≤60, prop ≤63). Prefs props are class-namespaced, so only tks_-prefixed prefs props are infix-checked (bare auto_* / confirm_* out of scope — avoids ~400 false positives). Sentinel # NAME-OK: <reason> (reuses crash_06's _s_line_has_sentinel). Allow-list seeded from §4.2 + log / warn / assign (real logging prefs + the tks_warn_expand_* / tks_assign_expand_* dynamic families the §4.2 prose named but its grouped lists omitted — §4.2 updated in lockstep per §10). PG/mixin descriptor check strips an optional feature infix (fixed TKS_VSW_* PropertyGroups false-flagging non-PascalCase). Wired into rules.py (INFO-05, INFO/INFO/none, sentinel NAME-OK), state.py (naming_* metrics), report.py (dispatch after INFO-04, ## INFO-05 markdown section, DATA.parts['INFO-05'] JSON block with by_rule breakdown), js/app.js (HUMAN_CONTENT['INFO-05'], icon type). Informational only — surfaces the §11 migration backlog without re-baselining any score. Real result: 43 findings = exactly the §11 backlog (9 TKS_MT_create_*_preset + 8 TKS_PT_*_presets_popover snake descriptors, 2 TKS_OT_smart_undo/redo, 13 un-prefixed *PropsMixin, 5 ops_-prefix gaps, 4 NAME-05 word-collision idnames, 2 TKS_PG_* fake-infix). Tests dev/tests/test_naming_conformance.py (43; via Blender headless or dev/scripts/run_naming_tests.py in plain CPython — conftest's autouse bpy fixture blocks bare pytest). OPEN: maintainer triage of the 43 (fix vs # NAME-OK).
    8. Legacy Part A..Z audit-letter scheme eliminated — every check is its category ID end-to-end. rules.py drops the legacy field + BY_LEGACY + rule_for_legacy (the rule ID is the sole identity). report.py's parts dict is re-keyed to rule IDs ('S'→'CRASH-06', 'M'→'REG-07', 'SPEED'→'PERF-02', 'COMPAT'→'CORR-03', …); the taxonomy overlay simplified to BY_ID.get(id) (dropped legacy_part + legacy_map); the markdown Audit-Taxonomy table lost its "Was" column; 190 prose Part <token> comments across state.py / visitor.py / cli.py / tests_perf.py / parts/*.py rewritten to IDs. js/app.js: HUMAN_CONTENT re-keyed to IDs (the two non-rule overview cards → 'COMPOSITION' / 'QUALITY'), partCode() fallback no longer prepends "Part ", CATEGORIES maps via r.id; letter-flavoured part-key identifiers renamed (letters→partKeys, orderedLetters→orderedPartKeys, .letters group prop →.keys, letter / partLetter(s) params →partKey; terse loop var L left as a conventional counter). Migrator dev/scripts/migrate_legacy_part_scheme.py; docs (ROADMAP.md, reports/README.md, reports/other/*, 4 troubleshooting docs) + the maintainer memory swept too. Follow-up fix (same unreleased change, never shipped broken): the SPEED→PERF-02 re-key left three bespoke speed renderers reading DATA.parts.SPEED via dot-access (overview speed tile, recommendations, renderSpeedTable) — missed by the migrator's scoped patterns and by quoted/bracket greps — so the Speed card + breakdown rendered "Not measured" until all three were pointed at DATA.parts['PERF-02']; regression guard dev/scripts/verify_part_key_refs.py asserts every hardcoded DATA.parts.<key> resolves to a real data key; doc doc/troubleshooting/stats_speed_card_not_measured_after_rekey.md. Verified: all 26 part keys are IDs, zero legacy in the taxonomy, INFO-05/CRASH-06/PERF-02 stamped, node --check clean, 132 engine tests pass in Blender (naming + preset-dispatch + manual-map + channel-coverage).

    Added¶

    1. 🟢 Keyframe pies gain Still and Animation sub-modes with scope. Six configurable pies — {kf_pie, kf_alt_pie} × {main, still, anim} — on the existing slot-enum system. Sub-pie menus TKS_MT_PIE_Keyframe{Still,Anim,ClearStill,ClearAnim} render through _draw_pie_from_slots. _SLOT_ACTION_MAP (panels/pie_menus/keyframe.py) reworked from 3- to 4-tuples (op_idname, props_dict, label, icon) so a slot can carry scope / whole_timeline / menu name; OPEN_STILL / OPEN_ANIMATION (+_CLEAR) map to wm.call_menu_pie and are gated in _draw_pie_from_slots by their kf_*_enabled toggle. Added 27 expand_* BoolProperty flags to LoggingPropsMixin (props/props_logging.py), default=True so previously-flat panels stay visible post-conversion. New draw_accordion_chevron helper for collapsibles with extra header widgets (Topics enable-checkbox, Tokens invalid-count badge). AddonPreferences draw() is not exercised by the suite (needs a live UI region); visual verification pending an in-app restart.
    2. 🟢 Shift+Click any section chevron to expand or collapse the whole menu at once. New TKS_OT_ToggleAccordion (tks.toggle_accordion, bl_options={'INTERNAL'}) in preferences/ops_misc.py with a single target: StringProperty. invoke() reads event.shift: on a plain click it toggles only target; on Shift+Click it finds the menu group containing target in the ACCORDION_GROUPS registry (addon_prefs_constants.py — one tuple per Preferences sub-tab) and sets every flag in that group to the clicked section's new state (falls back to a single-target toggle if target isn't registered). The chevron is rendered as this operator (emboss=False) inside draw_collapsible_section and draw_accordion_chevron, so every accordion inherits Shift+Click-all with no per-call wiring. (0.7.8: invoke now routes through the pure _accordion_new_states helper to also support accordion_solo_mode — see Added #4.)
    3. 🟢 Single mode-aware render control replaces the two FG/BG menu buttons. Removed TKS_MT_BatchRenderForegroundMenu / TKS_MT_BatchRenderBackgroundMenu and _BATCH_DROPDOWN_ACTIONS. New TKS_MT_RenderMenu dropdown: a wm.tks_render_mode Foreground/Background toggle drawn via wm.context_set_enum operator buttons with CHECKBOX_HLT/CHECKBOX_DEHLT icons (prop_enum was rejected — it draws a radio dot and ignores custom icons); scopes categorized SELECTED TAKES / ALL TAKES / OTHER via a dimmed single-label _category_label helper (a split icon cell staircased the dropdown columns — reverted); each _scope_row appends a _scope_task_count computed via _build_task_list only on menu open.     Removed¶

    1. 🟢 Reset Camera Visibility button removed from the TKS_OT_IconVisibilitySettings draw. The operator class TKS_OT_ResetCameraVisibility and core _reset_camera_visibility are retained — the latter is still used by the automations update callback (props/props_automations.py).
